local PhaseOrJetfarmToggle = Tabs.Welcome:AddToggle("PhaseOrJetfarm", {
    Title = "Auto Bring All Orbs/Slapple/Toolbox",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.PhaseOrJetfarm = Value

        task.spawn(function()
            while _G.PhaseOrJetfarm do
                for _, v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.Name == "JetOrb" or v.Name == "PhaseOrb" or v.Name == "GlitchOrb" or v.Name == "SiphonOrb" or v.Name == "MaterializeOrb" or v.Name == "Slapple" or v.Name == "GoldenSlapple" or v.Name == "Toolbox" then
                        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if character then
                            local head = character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                            if head then
                                firetouchinterest(head, v, 0)
                                firetouchinterest(head, v, 1)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                task.wait()
            end
        end)
    end
})

local AutoMegarockToggle = Tabs.MEGAROCK:AddToggle("AutoMegarock", {
    Title = "Auto Get MEGAROCK Glove",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Diamond" and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(10001, -42, 10000)
                task.wait(0.5)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Rockmode:FireServer()
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Diamond Glove/Use In Arena",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                task.wait(0.05)
                AutoMegarockToggle:SetValue(false)
            end
        end
    end
})

local AntiAfkToggle = Tabs.MEGAROCK:AddToggle("AntiAfk", {
    Title = "Anti Afk",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AntiAfk = Value
        local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')

        game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
            VirtualUser:CaptureController()
            VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
        end)
    end
})

-- Plague Tab
Tabs.Plague:AddButton({
    Title = "Someone Using Plague?",
    Callback = function()
        local found = false

        for _, player in ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "Plague" then
                    found = true
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Detected!",
                        Content = player.Name .. " has equipped the Plague glove.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                end
            end
        end

        if not found then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "No one has equipped the Plague glove",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Plague:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Plague Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Plague" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))

            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Duration = 3
            })
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Plague Player Not Found",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Hallow Jack Tab
Tabs.HallowJack:AddButton({
    Title = "Equip Killstreak (5k+ Slaps Need)",
    Callback = function()
        fireclickdetector(workspace.Lobby["Killstreak"].ClickDetector)
    end
})

Tabs.HallowJack:AddButton({
    Title = "Killstreak Slap Aura",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Killstreak" then
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            while true do
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") then
                        local args = {
                            [1] = player.Character["Right Arm"]
                        }
                        ReplicatedStorage.KSHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                    end
                end
                wait(0.5)
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Killstreak",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

if not game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("Gravestone") then
    GraveSpawn = Tabs.HallowJack:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Grave Status",
        Content = "Detected Grave: [ No ]"
    })
else
    GraveSpawn = Tabs.HallowJack:AddParagraph({
        Title = "Grave Status",
        Content = "Detected Grave: [ Yes ]"
    })
end

local AutoSetInfoToggle = Tabs.HallowJack:AddToggle("AutoSetInfo", {
    Title = "Auto Set Gravestone Info",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AutoSetInfo = Value
        local AutoSetInfoServer = game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Connect(function()
            if _G.AutoSetInfo == true then
                if not game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("Gravestone") then
                    GraveSpawn:SetText("Detected Grave: [ No ]")
                else
                    GraveSpawn:SetText("Detected Grave: [ Yes ]")
                end
            elseif _G.AutoSetInfo == false then
                if AutoSetInfoServer then
                    AutoSetInfoServer:Disconnect()
                    AutoSetInfoServer = nil
                end
            end
        end)
    end
})

local GraveESPToggle = Tabs.HallowJack:AddToggle("GraveESP", {
    Title = "Grave ESP",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        GraveESP = Value

        if not Value then
            local grave = workspace:FindFirstChild("Gravestone")
            if grave and grave:IsA("Model") then
                local gui = grave:FindFirstChild("GraveESP")
                if gui then gui:Destroy() end
            end
            return
        end

        task.spawn(function()
            while GraveESP do
                local lp = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                local char = lp.Character
                local hrp = char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

                if hrp then
                    local graveTarget = workspace:FindFirstChild("Gravestone")
                    if graveTarget and graveTarget:IsA("Model") then
                        local gui = graveTarget:FindFirstChild("GraveESP")

                        if not gui then
                            gui = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
                            gui.Name = "GraveESP"
                            gui.Adornee = graveTarget
                            gui.Size = UDim2.new(0, 150, 0, 40)
                            gui.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                            gui.AlwaysOnTop = true
                            gui.Parent = graveTarget

                            local label = Instance.new("TextLabel", gui)
                            label.Name = "Label"
                            label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
                            label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
                            label.TextSize = 16
                            label.Font = Enum.Font.FredokaOne
                            label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
                            label.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.2
                            label.Text = "Grave"
                        end

                        local label = gui:FindFirstChild("Label")
                        if label then
                            local dist = math.floor((graveTarget:GetPivot().Position - hrp.Position).Magnitude)
                            label.Text = "Grave | " .. dist .. "m"
                        end
                    end
                end
                task.wait(0.5)
            end
        end)
    end
})

Tabs.HallowJack:AddButton({
    Title = "Click On Grave",
    Callback = function()
        fireclickdetector(workspace.Gravestone.ClickDetector)
    end
})

-- [REDACTED] Tab
Tabs.REDACTED:AddButton({
    Title = "Get [Redacted] Glove",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Slaps.Value >= 0 then
            Door = 0
            for i = 1, 10 do
                Door = Door + 1
                if game:GetService("BadgeService"):UserHasBadgeAsync(game.Players.LocalPlayer.UserId, 2124847850) then
                    Door = nil
                else
                    firetouchinterest(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Head"), workspace.PocketDimension.Doors[Door].TouchInterest.Parent, 0)
                    firetouchinterest(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Head"), workspace.PocketDimension.Doors[Door].TouchInterest.Parent, 1)
                    wait(3.75)
                end
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "0+ Slaps Required",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.bus:AddButton({
    Title = "Someone Using bus?",
    Callback = function()

        for _, player in ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "bus" then
                    found = true
                    Fluent:Notify({

                    })
                end
            end

                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end

Tabs.bus:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To bus Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "bus" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then

            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))

                Duration = 3
            })
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "bus Player Not Found",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Warp Tab
Tabs.Warp:AddButton({
    Title = "Get Warp Glove",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Swapper" and not game:GetService("BadgeService"):UserHasBadgeAsync(game.Players.LocalPlayer.UserId, 0) then
            if _G.ClosestMagnitude == nil then
                _G.ClosestMagnitude = 999999
            end
            repeat
                for _, v in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if v ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and v.Character and v.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and v.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
                        local Magnitude = (game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - v.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                        if Magnitude <= _G.ClosestMagnitude then
                            if v.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") == nil or v.Character.Humanoid.Health == 0 then
                                _G.ClosestMagnitude = 999999
                                RandomPlayer = nil
                            else
                                _G.ClosestMagnitude = Magnitude
                                RandomPlayer = v
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                if RandomPlayer and _G.ClosestMagnitude ~= 999999 then
                    if RandomPlayer ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and RandomPlayer.Character then
                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") and RandomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") and RandomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and RandomPlayer.Character.Ragdolled.Value == false then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = RandomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Head").CFrame
                            wait(0.17)
                            game.ReplicatedStorage.HitSwapper:FireServer(RandomPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Head"))
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace["SafeBox"].CFrame * CFrame.new(0,5,0)
                        end
                    end
                end
                task.wait(0.15)
            until RandomPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position.Y < -10
            wait(0.2)
            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = RandomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart").CFrame * CFrame.new(0,10,0)
            wait(0.15)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").SLOC:FireServer()
            wait(0.2)
            if _G.ClosestMagnitude and RandomPlayer then
                _G.ClosestMagnitude = nil
                RandomPlayer = nil
            end
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Swapper",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Bomb Tab
Tabs.Bomb:AddButton({
    Title = "Get Bomb Glove",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Warp" and not game:GetService("BadgeService"):UserHasBadgeAsync(game.Players.LocalPlayer.UserId, 0) then
            OldTouch = workspace.DEATHBARRIER.CanTouch
            local players = game.Players:GetChildren()
            local RandomPlayer = players[math.random(1, #players)]
            repeat RandomPlayer = players[math.random(1, #players)] until RandomPlayer ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and RandomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") and RandomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled").Value == false
            Target = RandomPlayer
            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = Target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart").CFrame
            task.wait(0.2)
            game.ReplicatedStorage.WarpHt:FireServer(Target.Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart"))
            task.wait(0.15)
            if workspace.DEATHBARRIER.CanTouch == true then
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = game:GetService("Workspace").DEATHBARRIER.CFrame
                workspace.DEATHBARRIER.CanTouch = true
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = game:GetService("Workspace").DEATHBARRIER.CFrame
            end
            wait(0.1)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").WLOC:FireServer()
            wait(0.2)
            workspace.DEATHBARRIER.CanTouch = OldTouch
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Warp",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Bubble Tab
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
_G.KillstreakSlapRunning = false

local KillstreakSlapToggle = Tabs.Bubble:AddToggle("KillstreakSlap", {
    Title = "Auto Slap Players (Killstreak)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.KillstreakSlapRunning = state

        local function teleportToRandomPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            if #playerList > 1 then
                local randomPlayer
                repeat
                    randomPlayer = playerList[math.random(1, #playerList)]
                until randomPlayer ~= LocalPlayer

                local char = randomPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                end
            end
        end

        local function fireKSHitForAllPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                    if rightArm then
                        ReplicatedStorage.KSHit:FireServer(rightArm)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function runAutoSlapKillstreakLoop()
            if LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value ~= "Killstreak" then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Killstreak glove.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                _G.KillstreakSlapRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.KillstreakSlapRunning do
                wait(0.5)
                teleportToRandomPlayer()
                fireKSHitForAllPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoSlapKillstreakLoop)()
        else
            _G.KillstreakSlapRunning = false
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Bubble:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Killstreak Slap Aura",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Killstreak" then
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            while true do
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") then
                        local args = {
                            [1] = player.Character["Right Arm"]
                        }
                        ReplicatedStorage.KSHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                    end
                end
                wait(0.5)
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Killstreak",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

local DisarmSlapToggle = Tabs.Bubble:AddToggle("DisarmSlap", {
    Title = "Auto Slap Players (Reaper)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.DisarmSlapRunning = state

        local function teleportToRandomPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            if #playerList > 1 then
                local randomPlayer
                repeat
                    randomPlayer = playerList[math.random(1, #playerList)]
                until randomPlayer ~= LocalPlayer

                    local localHRP = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function fireReaperHitForAllPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                    if rightArm then
                        ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("ReaperHit"):FireServer(rightArm)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function runAutoDisarmSlapLoop()
            local leaderstats = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

            if not (glove and glove.Value == "Reaper") then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Reaper glove.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                _G.DisarmSlapRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.DisarmSlapRunning do
                task.wait(0.5)
                teleportToRandomPlayer()
                fireReaperHitForAllPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoDisarmSlapLoop)()
        else
            _G.DisarmSlapRunning = false
        end
    end
})

_G.SnowOverkillRunning = false

local SnowOverkillToggle = Tabs.Shard:AddToggle("SnowOverkill", {
    Title = "Auto Slap OVERKILL Players (Snow)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.SnowOverkillRunning = state

        local function teleportToOverkillPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            local overkillPlayers = {}

            for _, player in pairs(playerList) do
                if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                    local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                    local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                    if glove and glove.Value == "OVERKILL" then
                        table.insert(overkillPlayers, player)
                    end
                end
            end

            if #overkillPlayers > 0 then
                local randomPlayer = overkillPlayers[math.random(1, #overkillPlayers)]
                local char = randomPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local localHRP = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function fireSnowHitForOverkillPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                    local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                    local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                    if glove and glove.Value == "OVERKILL" and player.Character then
                        local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                        if rightArm then
                            ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("SnowHit"):FireServer(rightArm)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function runAutoSnowOverkillLoop()
            local leaderstats = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

            if not (glove and glove.Value == "Snow") then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Snow glove.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                _G.SnowOverkillRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.SnowOverkillRunning do
                task.wait(0.5)
                teleportToOverkillPlayer()
                fireSnowHitForOverkillPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoSnowOverkillLoop)()
        else
            _G.SnowOverkillRunning = false
        end
    end
})

    Title = "Auto Snow Slap Aura (OVERKILL Players Only)",

            for i = 1, 75000 do
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Duplicate:FireServer(unpack({[1] = true}))
            end
            wait(2)
            loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Jelly-plays/Rejoin-script/main/obf_L744By559M18BbuseSG6en8r1zL31daK9060LV7WyvmS4bQp92aONWfwRE36FdcZ.lua.txt"))()

                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end

Tabs.buddies:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Slap Aura Players",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Golden" then
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            while true do
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do

                        local args = {
                            [1] = player.Character["Left Leg"],
                            [2] = false
                        }
                        ReplicatedStorage.GoldenHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                    end
                end
                wait(0.5)
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Golden",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Jupiter Tab
Tabs.Jupiter:AddButton({
    Title = "Someone Using God's Hand?",
    Callback = function()
        local found = false

        for _, player in ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "God's Hand" then
                    found = true
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Detected!",
                        Content = player.Name .. " has equipped the God's Hand glove.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                end
            end
        end

        if not found then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "No one has equipped the God's Hand glove",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Jupiter:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To God's Hand Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "God's Hand" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))

            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Duration = 3
            })
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "God's Hand Player Not Found",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

local JupiterAntiRagdollToggle = Tabs.Jupiter:AddToggle("JupiterAntiRagdoll", {
    Title = "Anti Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AntiRagdoll = Value
        while _G.AntiRagdoll do
            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") then
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Ragdolled").Value == true then
                    repeat task.wait()
                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.Anchored = true
                        end
                    until game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Ragdolled").Value == false
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") then
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.Anchored = false
                    end
                end
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end
})

-- Rage Tab
Tabs.Rage:AddButton({
    Title = "Equip Default (0+ Slaps Need)",
    Callback = function()
        fireclickdetector(workspace.Lobby["Default"].ClickDetector)
    end
})

_G.AutoSlapRunning = false

local AutoSlapToggle = Tabs.Rage:AddToggle("AutoSlap", {
    Title = "Auto Slap Players (50+ Killstreak Users Only)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.AutoSlapRunning = state

        local function hasDefaultGlove()
            local leaderstats = game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "Default" then
                    return true
                end
            end
            return false
        end

        local function findPlayerWith50Plus()
            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                if player ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and player.Character then
                    local head = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                    if head then
                        local nametag = head:FindFirstChild("Nametag")
                        if nametag then
                            local labels = nametag:FindFirstChild("Labels")
                            if labels then
                                local topLabel = labels:FindFirstChild("TopLabel")
                                if topLabel and topLabel:IsA("TextLabel") and topLabel.Text then
                                    local numbers = string.match(topLabel.Text, "%d+")
                                    if numbers then
                                        local numberValue = tonumber(numbers)
                                        if numberValue and numberValue >= 50 then
                                            return player
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            return nil
        end

        local function teleportToTargetPlayer()
            local targetPlayer = findPlayerWith50Plus()
            if targetPlayer then
                local char = targetPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local localChar = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                    local localHRP = localChar and localChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                        return true
                    end
                end
            end
            return false
        end

        local function fireRemoteForAllPlayers()
            local remote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("b")
            if not remote then
                return
            end

            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                    if rightArm then
                        pcall(function()
                            remote:FireServer(rightArm)
                        end)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function runAutoSlapLoop()
            if not hasDefaultGlove() then
                _G.AutoSlapRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.AutoSlapRunning do
                if not hasDefaultGlove() then
                    _G.AutoSlapRunning = false
                    break
                end

                task.wait(0.5)
                local teleported = teleportToTargetPlayer()
                fireRemoteForAllPlayers()

                if not teleported then
                    task.wait(2)
                end
            end
        end

        if state then
            if hasDefaultGlove() then
                coroutine.wrap(runAutoSlapLoop)()
            else
                _G.AutoSlapRunning = false
            end
        else
            _G.AutoSlapRunning = false
        end
    end  -- THIS WAS MISSING
})  -- THIS WAS MISSING

    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)

        while SlappleFarm do

                for _, v in pairs(workspace.Arena.island5.Slapples:GetChildren()) do
                    local plrChar = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                    if plrChar and plrChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and plrChar:FindFirstChild("entered") then
                        if (v.Name == "Slapple" or v.Name == "GoldenSlapple") and v:FindFirstChild("Glove") and v.Glove:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TouchTransmitter") then
                            firetouchinterest(plrChar.HumanoidRootPart, v.Glove, 0)
                            firetouchinterest(plrChar.HumanoidRootPart, v.Glove, 1)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end

-- Disarm Tab
_G.DisarmSlapRunning = false

local DisarmSlapToggle2 = Tabs.Disarm:AddToggle("DisarmSlap2", {
    Title = "Auto Slap Players (Reaper)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.DisarmSlapRunning = state

        local function teleportToRandomPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            if #playerList > 1 then
                local randomPlayer
                repeat
                    randomPlayer = playerList[math.random(1, #playerList)]
                until randomPlayer ~= LocalPlayer

                local char = randomPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local localHRP = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function fireReaperHitForAllPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                    if rightArm then
                        ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("ReaperHit"):FireServer(rightArm)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function runAutoDisarmSlapLoop()
            local leaderstats = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

            if not (glove and glove.Value == "Reaper") then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Reaper glove.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                _G.DisarmSlapRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.DisarmSlapRunning do
                task.wait(0.5)
                teleportToRandomPlayer()
                fireReaperHitForAllPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoDisarmSlapLoop)()
        else
            _G.DisarmSlapRunning = false
        end
    end
})

    Title = "Auto Reaper Slap Aura",
    Callback = function()

{
    Title = "Choose Option To Auto Collect Candy Corns",
    Description = "Select Teleport to move to candy corns or Bring to bring them to you",
    Values = {"Teleport", "Bring"},
    Multi = false,
    Default = "Teleport",
    Callback = function(Value)
        CandyCornCollector = Value
        print("Candy corn collector mode changed to:", Value) -- Optional debug
    end
})

local AutoCollectCandyCornsToggle = Tabs.Rattlebones:AddToggle("AutoCollectCandyCorns", {
    Title = "Auto Collect Candy Corns",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        AutoCollectCandyCorns = Value

        if Value then
            if hasNecromancerBadge() then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Already Have Badge",
                    Content = "You already have Necromancer glove badge! The farm will not work.",
                    Duration = 5
                })
                AutoCollectCandyCorns = false
                AutoCollectCandyCornsToggle:SetValue(false)
                return
            end

            if CandyCornCollector == "Teleport" then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while AutoCollectCandyCorns do
                        if hasNecromancerBadge() then
                            Fluent:Notify({
                                Title = "Badge Obtained!",
                                Content = "You got the Necromancer glove badge! Farm stopped.",
                                Duration = 5
                            })
                            AutoCollectCandyCorns = false
                            AutoCollectCandyCornsToggle:SetValue(false)
                            break
                        end

                        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            local foundCandyCorn = false

                            for _, part in pairs(workspace.CandyCorns:GetChildren()) do
                                if not AutoCollectCandyCorns then break end

                                if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                                    foundCandyCorn = true
                                    character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(part.Position + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0))
                                    task.wait(0.2)
                                    break
                                end
                            end

                            if not foundCandyCorn then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end
                        end
                        task.wait()
                    end
                end)
            elseif CandyCornCollector == "Bring" then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while AutoCollectCandyCorns do
                        if hasNecromancerBadge() then
                            Fluent:Notify({
                                Title = "Badge Obtained!",
                                Content = "You got the Necromancer glove badge! Farm stopped.",
                                Duration = 5
                            })
                            AutoCollectCandyCorns = false
                            AutoCollectCandyCornsToggle:SetValue(false)
                            break
                        end

                        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            local humanoidRootPart = character.HumanoidRootPart

                            for _, part in pairs(workspace.CandyCorns:GetChildren()) do
                                if not AutoCollectCandyCorns then break end

                                if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                                    part.CFrame = humanoidRootPart.CFrame
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    end
})

local AutoTycoonToggle = Tabs.Tycoon:AddToggle("AutoTycoon", {
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Plate",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AutoTpPlate = Value
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") and #game.Players:GetPlayers() >= 7 then
            while _G.AutoTpPlate do
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") and #game.Players:GetPlayers() >= 7 then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = game.workspace.Arena.Plate.CFrame
                end
                task.wait()
            end
        elseif _G.AutoTpPlate == true then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "You Need Enter Arena/7 People In Server Required",
                Duration = 3
            })
            wait(0.05)
            AutoTycoonToggle:SetValue(false)
        end
    end
})

-- Confusion Tab
Tabs.Confusion:AddButton({
    Title = "Equip spin (-3+ Slaps Need)",
    Callback = function()
        fireclickdetector(workspace.Lobby["spin"].ClickDetector)
    end
})

Tabs.Confusion:AddButton({
    Title = "Someone Using Reaper?",
    Callback = function()
        local found = false

        for _, player in ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "Reaper" then
                    found = true
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Detected!",
                        Content = player.Name .. " has equipped the Reaper glove.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                end
            end
        end

        if not found then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "No one has equipped the Reaper glove",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Confusion:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Reaper Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Reaper" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))

            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Duration = 3
            })
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Reaper Player Not Found",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Confusion:AddButton({
    Title = "Destroy All Tycoons",
    Callback = function()
        for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
            if string.find(v.Name, "ÅTycoon") then
                local clickPart = v:FindFirstChild("Destruct")
                if clickPart and clickPart:IsA("BasePart") then
                    local detector = clickPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("ClickDetector")
                    if detector then
                        fireclickdetector(detector)
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

local ConfusionGiftfarmToggle = Tabs.Confusion:AddToggle("ConfusionGiftfarm", {
    Title = "Auto Bring Bus",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        Giftfarm = Value
        while Giftfarm do
            for i,v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                if v.Name == "BusModel" then
                    firetouchinterest(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart"), v, 0)
                    firetouchinterest(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart"), v, 1)
                end
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end
})

local GlitchfarmToggle = Tabs.Glitch:AddToggle("Glitchfarm", {
    Title = "Auto Slap Phase/Jet Orb + Auto Touch Glitch Orb",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Error" then
            _G.Glitchfarm = Value

            while _G.Glitchfarm do
                local glove = game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove
                if glove and glove.Value == "Error" then
                    local jetOrb = game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("JetOrb")
                    local phaseOrb = game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("PhaseOrb")

                    if jetOrb then
                        game.ReplicatedStorage.Errorhit:FireServer(jetOrb)
                    end
                    if phaseOrb then
                        game.ReplicatedStorage.Errorhit:FireServer(phaseOrb)
                    end
                else
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Equip Error",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                end
                task.wait(1)
            end
        end
    end
})

local SnowballGiftfarmToggle = Tabs.Snowball:AddToggle("SnowballGiftfarm", {
    Title = "Auto Bring Gift",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        Giftfarm = Value
        while Giftfarm do
            for i,v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                if v.Name == "Gift" then
                    firetouchinterest(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart"), v, 0)
                    firetouchinterest(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart"), v, 1)
                end
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end
})

-- Elude Tab
Tabs.Elude:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Teleport To ? Place + Auto TP To Glove",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 11828384869
        local targetPosition = Vector3.new(-503, 19, -179)
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId
        local isReExecution = false

        local function teleportToPosition()
            local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
            if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPosition)
            end
        end

        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local teleportScript = [[
                        wait(2)
                        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(-503, 19, -179))
                        end
                    ]]

                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(teleportScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(teleportScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            if isReExecution then
                teleportToPosition()
            else
                teleportToPosition()
                setupTeleportMonitor()
            end
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId)
            end)
            if not success and connection then
                connection:Disconnect()
            end
        end
    end
})

-- RNG Tab
_G.DiceSlapRunning = false

local DiceSlapToggle = Tabs.RNG:AddToggle("DiceSlap", {
    Title = "Auto Slap Players",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.DiceSlapRunning = state

        local function teleportToRandomPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            if #playerList > 1 then
                local randomPlayer
                repeat
                    randomPlayer = playerList[math.random(1, #playerList)]
                until randomPlayer ~= LocalPlayer

                local char = randomPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local localHRP = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function fireDiceHitForAllPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                    if rightArm then
                        ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("DiceHit"):FireServer(rightArm)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function runAutoDiceSlapLoop()
            local leaderstats = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

            if not (glove and glove.Value == "Dice") then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Dice glove.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                _G.DiceSlapRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.DiceSlapRunning do
                task.wait(0.5)
                teleportToRandomPlayer()
                fireDiceHitForAllPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoDiceSlapLoop)()
        else
            _G.DiceSlapRunning = false
        end
    end
})

Tabs.RNG:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Dice Slap Aura",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Dice" then
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            while true do
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") then
                        local args = {
                            [1] = player.Character.Head
                        }
                        ReplicatedStorage.DiceHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                    end
                end
                wait(0.5)
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Dice",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- fish Tab
Tabs.fish:AddButton({
    Title = "Create Safespot",
    Callback = function()
        if workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot") == nil then
            local Safespot = Instance.new("Model", workspace)
            Safespot.Name = "Safespot"

            local base = Instance.new("Part")
            base.Name = "Base"
            base.Size = Vector3.new(500, 10, 500)
            base.Position = Vector3.new(10000, -50, 10000)
            base.Anchored = true
            base.CanCollide = true
            base.Transparency = 0.5
            base.Parent = Safespot

            local partsData = {
                {"DefendPart",  Vector3.new(500, 117, 5),   Vector3.new(10000.2, 13, 9752.45)},
                {"DefendPart1", Vector3.new(5, 117, 496),   Vector3.new(10248.2, 13, 10002.4)},
                {"DefendPart2", Vector3.new(497, 117, 6),   Vector3.new(9998.13, 13, 10247.2)},
                {"DefendPart3", Vector3.new(7, 117, 490),   Vector3.new(9752.71, 13, 9999.28)},
                {"DefendPart4", Vector3.new(491, 10, 491),  Vector3.new(10001.1, 76, 9999.66)},
            }

            for _, partInfo in pairs(partsData) do
                local part = Instance.new("Part")
                part.Name = partInfo[1]
                part.Size = partInfo[2]
                part.Position = partInfo[3]
                part.Anchored = true
                part.CanCollide = true
                part.Transparency = 0.5
                part.Parent = Safespot
            end
        end

        Fluent:Notify({
            Title = "Checker",
            Content = "Created Successfully!",
            Duration = 3
        })
    end
})

Tabs.fish:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Get fish Glove",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "ZZZZZZZ" and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
            wait(0.5)
            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(10001, -42, 10000)
            wait(1)
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("ZZZZZZZSleep"):FireServer()
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip ZZZZZZZ",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Goofy:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Confusion Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Confusion" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end

            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))

            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success!",

                Duration = 3
            })
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Confusion Player Not Found",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Leash:AddButton({
    Title = "Someone Using CULT?",
    Callback = function()
        local found = false

        for _, player in ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "CULT" then
                    found = true
                    Fluent:Notify({

_G.BoomerangHOverkillRunning = false

local BoomerangHOverkillToggle = Tabs.Flamarang:AddToggle("BoomerangHOverkill",  -- Added unique key
{
    Title = "Auto Slap OVERKILL Players (Boomerang)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.BoomerangHOverkillRunning = state

        local function teleportToOverkillPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            local overkillPlayers = {}

            for _, player in pairs(playerList) do
                if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                    local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                    local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                    if glove and glove.Value == "OVERKILL" then
                        table.insert(overkillPlayers, player)
                    end
                end
            end

            if #overkillPlayers > 0 then
                local randomPlayer = overkillPlayers[math.random(1, #overkillPlayers)]
                local char = randomPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local localHRP = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function fireBoomerangHForOverkillPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                    local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                    local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                    if glove and glove.Value == "OVERKILL" and player.Character then
                        local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                        if rightArm then
                            ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("BoomerangH"):FireServer(rightArm)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function runAutoBoomerangHOverkillLoop()
            local leaderstats = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

            if not (glove and glove.Value == "Boomerang") then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Boomerang glove.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                _G.BoomerangHOverkillRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.BoomerangHOverkillRunning do
                task.wait(0.5)
                teleportToOverkillPlayer()
                fireBoomerangHForOverkillPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoBoomerangHOverkillLoop)()
        else
            _G.BoomerangHOverkillRunning = false
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Flamarang:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Boomerang Slap Aura (OVERKILL Players Only)",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Boomerang" then
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            while true do
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                        local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                        local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

                        if glove and glove.Value == "OVERKILL" and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") then
                            local args = {
                                [1] = player.Character["Left Arm"]
                            }
                            ReplicatedStorage.BoomerangH:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end
                end
                wait(0.5)
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Boomerang",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Kinetic Tab
Tabs.Kinetic:AddButton({
    Title = "Equip Stun (870+ Slaps Need)",
    Callback = function()
        fireclickdetector(workspace.Lobby["Stun"].ClickDetector)
    end
})

Tabs.Kinetic:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Get Kinetic Glove",
    Callback = function()
        wait(0.2)
        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(10001, -42, 10000)
        wait(0.2)
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Stun" and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
            OGL = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
            for i = 1,150 do
                game.ReplicatedStorage.SelfKnockback:FireServer({["Force"] = 0,["Direction"] = Vector3.new(0,0.01,0)})
                wait(0.05)
            end
            wait(1.5)
            repeat
                local players = game.Players:GetChildren()
                local RandomPlayer = players[math.random(1, #players)]
                repeat RandomPlayer = players[math.random(1, #players)] until RandomPlayer ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and RandomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") and RandomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("rock") == nil and RandomPlayer.Character.Head:FindFirstChild("UnoReverseCard") == nil and RandomPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Health ~= 0
                Target = RandomPlayer
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = Target.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,-20,0)
                wait(0.25)
                game.ReplicatedStorage.StunR:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Stun)
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = OGL
                wait(0.5)
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("EMPStunBadgeCounter") then
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Tip",
                        Content = "Counter Stun [ "..game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.EMPStunBadgeCounter.Value.." ]",
                        Duration = 5
                    })
                end
                wait(12.3)
            until game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("EMPStunBadgeCounter") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.EMPStunBadgeCounter.Value >= 50
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Stun",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

local BerserkAntiRagdollToggle = Tabs.Berserk:AddToggle("BerserkAntiRagdoll", {
    Title = "Anti Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AntiRagdoll = Value
        while _G.AntiRagdoll do
            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") then
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Ragdolled").Value == true then
                    repeat task.wait()
                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.Anchored = true
                        end
                    until game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Ragdolled").Value == false
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") then
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.Anchored = false
                    end
                end
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end
})

            local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "Home Run" then
                    found = true
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Detected!",
                        Content = player.Name .. " has equipped the Home Run glove.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                end
            end
        end

        if not found then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "No one has equipped the Home Run glove",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Quake:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To woah Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "woah" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))

            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Duration = 3
            })
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "woah Player Not Found",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Psycho:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Reverse Slap Aura (Reverse Players Only)",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Reverse" then
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            while true do
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                        local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                        local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

                        if glove and glove.Value == "Reverse" and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") then
                            local args = {
                                [1] = player.Character["Left Arm"]
                            }
                            ReplicatedStorage.ReverseHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end
                end
                wait(0.5)
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Reverse",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Psycho:AddButton({
    Title = "Get Psycho Glove",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("RepressedMemoriesMap") ~= nil then
            OGL = game.Workspace.RepressedMemoriesMap.Psychokinesis.Triggers.StartPsychoEvent.CFrame
            OGL1 = game.Workspace.RepressedMemoriesMap.Psychokinesis.Triggers.StopPsychoEvent.CFrame
            wait(5)
            game.Workspace.RepressedMemoriesMap.Psychokinesis.Triggers.StartPsychoEvent.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
            wait(5)
            game.Workspace.RepressedMemoriesMap.Psychokinesis.Triggers.StartPsychoEvent.CFrame = OGL
            wait(5)
            game.Workspace.RepressedMemoriesMap.Psychokinesis.Triggers.StopPsychoEvent.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
            wait(5)
            game.Workspace.RepressedMemoriesMap.Psychokinesis.Triggers.StopPsychoEvent.CFrame = OGL1
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Be In Limbo World",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Counter Tab
Tabs.Counter:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Teleport To ? Place + Auto Get Counter",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 11828384869
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        local function executeCounterScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
            if getgenv().AutoGetCounterExecuted then return end

            getgenv().AutoGetCounterExecuted = true

            if game.PlaceId == 11828384869 then
                for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v:IsA("ClickDetector") then
                        fireclickdetector(v)
                    end
                end

                local hrp = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
                hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(1000, 1000, 1000)
                task.wait(0.6)
                hrp.Anchored = true

                local Time = 120
                while Time > 0 do
                    local msg = Instance.new("Message", workspace)
                    msg.Text = "Time left to receive: " .. Time
                    task.wait(1)
                    Time -= 1
                    msg:Destroy()
                end

                task.wait(1.5)

                for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v:IsA("ClickDetector") then
                        fireclickdetector(v)
                    end
                end
            else
                local places = {
                    11520107397, 9015014224, 6403373529, 124596094333302
                }

                for _, id in ipairs(places) do
                    if game.PlaceId == id then
                        while task.wait() do
                            game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(11828384869)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local counterScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == 11828384869 then
                            for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if v:IsA("ClickDetector") then
                                    fireclickdetector(v)
                                end
                            end

                            local hrp = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(1000, 1000, 1000)
                            task.wait(0.6)
                            hrp.Anchored = true

                            local Time = 120
                            while Time > 0 do
                                local msg = Instance.new("Message", workspace)
                                msg.Text = "Time left to receive: " .. Time
                                task.wait(1)
                                Time -= 1
                                msg:Destroy()
                            end

                            task.wait(1.5)

                            for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if v:IsA("ClickDetector") then
                                    fireclickdetector(v)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    ]]

                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(counterScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(counterScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            executeCounterScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId)
            end)
            if not success and connection then
                connection:Disconnect()
            end
        end
    end
})

local ToolboxfarmToggle = Tabs.Hammer:AddToggle("Toolboxfarm",  -- Added unique key
{
    Title = "Auto Click On Toolbox",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        Toolboxfarm = Value
        while Toolboxfarm do
            if game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("Toolbox") then
                for i,v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v.Name == "Toolbox" and v:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                        fireclickdetector(v.ClickDetector, 0)
                        fireclickdetector(v.ClickDetector, 1)
                    end
                end
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end
})

local AutoTycoonToggle2 = Tabs.rob:AddToggle("AutoTycoon2", {
    Title = "Auto Click Tycoon",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AutoTycoon = Value

        while _G.AutoTycoon do
            for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                if string.find(v.Name, "ÅTycoon") then
                    local clickPart = v:FindFirstChild("Click")
                    if clickPart and clickPart:IsA("BasePart") then
                        local detector = clickPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("ClickDetector")
                        if detector then
                            fireclickdetector(detector)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Rhythm:AddButton({

Tabs.Rhythm:AddButton({
    Title = "Use Boogie Ability (at center)",
    Callback = function()
        local args = {

local AutoGeneralAbilityToggle = Tabs.Hitman:AddToggle("AutoGeneralAbility", {
    Title = "Auto Use Track Ability",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        getgenv().AutoGeneralAbility = Value

        if Value then
            getgenv().GeneralAbilityConnection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                if not getgenv().AutoGeneralAbility then
                    getgenv().GeneralAbilityConnection:Disconnect()
                    return
                end
                task.wait(13)
                if getgenv().AutoGeneralAbility then
                    pcall(function()
                        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GeneralAbility:FireServer()
                    end)
                end
            end)
        else
            if getgenv().GeneralAbilityConnection then
                getgenv().GeneralAbilityConnection:Disconnect()
            end
        end
    end
})
