-- Null Tab
Tabs.Null:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Null Zone Place + Get Null",
    Callback = function()
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        if currentPlaceId == 6403373529 then
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats.Glove and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Pan" then
                if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(18662, 2993, -298)
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Teleported!",
                        Content = "Pan user teleported to Null position",
                        Duration = 5
                    })
                end
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Pan glove first!",
                    Duration = 5
                })
            end

        elseif currentPlaceId == 14422118326 then
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(5458, -189, 1854)
                wait(2)
                if workspace:FindFirstChild("Model") and workspace.Model:FindFirstChild("Handle") and workspace.Model.Handle:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                    fireclickdetector(workspace.Model.Handle.ClickDetector)
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Success!",
                        Content = "Got Null glove!",
                        Duration = 5
                    })
                end
            end

        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Teleporting...",
                Content = "Going to Null Zone",
                Duration = 3
            })

            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(14422118326)
            end)

            if success then
                game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                    if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                        local nullScript = [[
                            wait(3)
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(5458, -189, 1854)
                                wait(2)
                                if workspace:FindFirstChild("Model") and workspace.Model:FindFirstChild("Handle") and workspace.Model.Handle:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                                    fireclickdetector(workspace.Model.Handle.ClickDetector)
                                end
                            end
                        ]]

                        if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                            syn.queue_on_teleport(nullScript)
                        else
                            queue_on_teleport(nullScript)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Teleport Failed",
                    Content = errorMsg,
                    Duration = 5
                })
            end
        end
    end
})

                    if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                        local tinkererScript = [[
                            wait(3)
                            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then

                                        break
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        ]]

                            syn.queue_on_teleport(tinkererScript)
                        else
                            queue_on_teleport(tinkererScript)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Teleport Failed",

                    Duration = 5
                })
            end

-- Necromancer Tab (Duplicate of Rattlebones, but keeping for organization)
local NecromancerCandyCornCollector = "Teleport"
local NecromancerAutoCollectCandyCorns = false

local NecromancerDropdown = Tabs.Necromancer:AddDropdown("NecromancerCandyCornDropdown", 
{
    Title = "Choose Option To Auto Collect Candy Corns",
    Description = "Select Teleport to move to candy corns or Bring to bring them to you",
    Values = {"Teleport", "Bring"},
    Multi = false,
    Default = "Teleport",
    Callback = function(Value)
        NecromancerCandyCornCollector = Value
        print("Necromancer candy corn mode changed to:", Value) -- Optional debug
    end
})

local AutoCollectCandyCornsToggle = Tabs.Necromancer:AddToggle("AutoCollectCandyCorns", {
    Title = "Auto Collect Candy Corns",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        AutoCollectCandyCorns = Value

        if Value then
            if hasNecromancerBadge() then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Already Have Badge",
                    Content = "You already have Necromancer glove badge! The farm will not work.",
                    Duration = 5
                })
                AutoCollectCandyCorns = false
                AutoCollectCandyCornsToggle:SetValue(false)
                return
            end

            if CandyCornCollector == "Teleport" then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while AutoCollectCandyCorns do
                        if hasNecromancerBadge() then
                            Fluent:Notify({
                                Title = "Badge Obtained!",
                                Content = "You got the Necromancer glove badge! Farm stopped.",
                                Duration = 5
                            })
                            AutoCollectCandyCorns = false
                            AutoCollectCandyCornsToggle:SetValue(false)
                            break
                        end

                        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            local foundCandyCorn = false

                            for _, part in pairs(workspace.CandyCorns:GetChildren()) do
                                if not AutoCollectCandyCorns then break end

                                if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                                    foundCandyCorn = true
                                    character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(part.Position + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0))
                                    task.wait(0.2)
                                    break
                                end
                            end

                            if not foundCandyCorn then
                                task.wait(0.5)
                            end
                        end
                        task.wait()
                    end
                end)
            elseif CandyCornCollector == "Bring" then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while AutoCollectCandyCorns do
                        if hasNecromancerBadge() then
                            Fluent:Notify({
                                Title = "Badge Obtained!",
                                Content = "You got the Necromancer glove badge! Farm stopped.",
                                Duration = 5
                            })
                            AutoCollectCandyCorns = false
                            AutoCollectCandyCornsToggle:SetValue(false)
                            break
                        end

                        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            local humanoidRootPart = character.HumanoidRootPart

                            for _, part in pairs(workspace.CandyCorns:GetChildren()) do
                                if not AutoCollectCandyCorns then break end

                                if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                                    part.CFrame = humanoidRootPart.CFrame
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    end
})

-- Alchemist Tab
_G.PlagueSlapRunning = false

local PlagueSlapToggle = Tabs.Alchemist:AddToggle("PlagueSlap", {
    Title = "Auto Slap Players",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        _G.PlagueSlapRunning = state

        local function teleportToRandomPlayer()
            local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
            if #playerList > 1 then
                local randomPlayer
                repeat
                    randomPlayer = playerList[math.random(1, #playerList)]
                until randomPlayer ~= LocalPlayer

                local char = randomPlayer.Character
                if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    local localHRP = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if localHRP then
                        localHRP.CFrame = char.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function firePlagueHitForAllPlayers()
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player.Character then
                    local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("RightHand")
                    if rightArm then
                        ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("PlagueHit"):FireServer(rightArm)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function runAutoPlagueSlapLoop()
            local leaderstats = LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            local glove = leaderstats and leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")

            if not (glove and glove.Value == "Plague") then
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Plague glove.",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                _G.PlagueSlapRunning = false
                return
            end

            while _G.PlagueSlapRunning do
                task.wait(0.5)
                teleportToRandomPlayer()
                firePlagueHitForAllPlayers()
            end
        end

        if state then
            coroutine.wrap(runAutoPlagueSlapLoop)()
        else
            _G.PlagueSlapRunning = false
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Alchemist:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Slap Aura Players",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Plague" then
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            while true do
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") then
                        local args = {
                            [1] = player.Character["Left Arm"]
                        }
                        ReplicatedStorage.PlagueHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                    end
                end
                wait(0.5)
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Plague",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Druid Tab
Tabs.Druid:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport to Gardens And Ghouls Place (NOT AUTO GET GLOVE)",
    Callback = function()
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local rep = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

        if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Alchemist" then
            rep.GeneralAbility:FireServer()

            local function mixItem(itemName, times)
                times = times or 1
                rep.Firework:InvokeServer()
                rep.AlchemistEvent:FireServer("AddItem", itemName)
                rep.AlchemistEvent:FireServer("EquipItem", itemName)
                for _ = 1, times do
                    rep.AlchemistEvent:FireServer("MixItem", itemName)
                end
            end

            mixItem("Wild Vine", 3)
            mixItem("Blood Rose", 1)
            mixItem("Dark Root", 1)
            mixItem("Elder Wood", 1)
            mixItem("Jade Stone", 1)

            rep.AlchemistEvent:FireServer("BrewPotion")
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Alchemist Glove",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Jester Tab
Tabs.Jester:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Random Player",
    Callback = function()
        local players = game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()
        local localPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer

        local otherPlayers = {}
        for _, player in pairs(players) do
            if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                table.insert(otherPlayers, player)
            end
        end

        if #otherPlayers > 0 then
            local randomPlayer = otherPlayers[math.random(1, #otherPlayers)]
            if randomPlayer.Character and randomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                local targetPosition = randomPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position
                localPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(targetPosition)
            end
        end
    end
})

-- Santa Tab
Tabs.Santa:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Jerry Boss Fight Place + Auto Get Santa",
    Callback = function()
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        if currentPlaceId == 6403373529 then
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            wait(0.2)
            local arena = workspace:FindFirstChild("Arena")
            if arena then
                local xmasSnowPeeps = arena:FindFirstChild("XmasSnowPeeps")
                if xmasSnowPeeps then
                    for _, peep in ipairs(xmasSnowPeeps:GetChildren()) do
                        if peep:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                            fireclickdetector(peep.ClickDetector)
                            wait(0.1)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            wait(0.2)
            if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(2, -5, 353)
            end

        elseif currentPlaceId == 95706409702231 then
            local function executeSecondPlaceScript()
                task.wait(20)
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-6, 21, -542)
                    _G.AntiAfk = true
                    local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
                    game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                        if _G.AntiAfk then
                            VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                            VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end
            executeSecondPlaceScript()
        end

        game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
            if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                local targetPlaceId = 95706409702231
                local teleportScript = [[
                    wait(5)
                    if game.PlaceId == ]] .. targetPlaceId .. [[ then
                        task.wait(20)
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-6, 21, -542)
                            _G.AntiAfk = true
                            local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
                            game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                                if _G.AntiAfk then
                                    VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                                    VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
                                end
                            end)
                        end
                    end
                ]]

                if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                    syn.queue_on_teleport(teleportScript)
                elseif queue_on_teleport then
                    queue_on_teleport(teleportScript)
                end
            end
        end)
    end
})

    Title = "Teleport To ? Place + Collect Alchemist Hood",
    Callback = function()
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        if currentPlaceId == 6403373529 then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Teleporting...",
                Content = "Going to ? place for Alchemist Hood",
                Duration = 3
            })

            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(11828384869)
            end)

            if success then
                game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                    if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                        local hoodScript = [[
                            wait(3)
                            local lp = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local hrp = lp.Character and lp.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local target = workspace:FindFirstChild("_ugcQuestObjectEludeHat")
                            if target and target:FindFirstChild("Handle") and hrp then
                                if hrp.Anchored then 
                                    hrp.Anchored = false
                                    task.wait(0.5) 
                                end
                                hrp.CFrame = target.Handle.CFrame
                            end
                        ]]

                        if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                            syn.queue_on_teleport(hoodScript)
                        else
                            queue_on_teleport(hoodScript)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Teleport Failed",
                    Content = errorMsg,
                    Duration = 5
                })
            end

        elseif currentPlaceId == 11828384869 then
            local lp = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local hrp = lp.Character and lp.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            local target = workspace:FindFirstChild("_ugcQuestObjectEludeHat")
            if target and target:FindFirstChild("Handle") and hrp then
                if hrp.Anchored then 
                    hrp.Anchored = false
                    task.wait(0.5) 
                end
                hrp.CFrame = target.Handle.CFrame
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Success!",
                    Content = "Got Alchemist Hood!",
                    Duration = 5
                })
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "Alchemist Hood not found!",
                    Duration = 5
                })
            end

        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Teleporting...",
                Content = "Going to ? place for Alchemist Hood",
                Duration = 3
            })

            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(11828384869)
            end)

            if success then
                game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                    if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                        local hoodScript = [[
                            wait(3)
                            local lp = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            local hrp = lp.Character and lp.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            local target = workspace:FindFirstChild("_ugcQuestObjectEludeHat")
                            if target and target:FindFirstChild("Handle") and hrp then
                                if hrp.Anchored then 
                                    hrp.Anchored = false
                                    task.wait(0.5) 
                                end
                                hrp.CFrame = target.Handle.CFrame
                            end
                        ]]

                        if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                            syn.queue_on_teleport(hoodScript)
                        else
                            queue_on_teleport(hoodScript)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            else
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Teleport Failed",
                    Content = errorMsg,
                    Duration = 5
                })
            end
        end
    end
})

-- Admin Tab
Tabs.Admin:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To The Staff Application Place (NOT AUTO GET GLOVE)",
    Callback = function()
        local firstPlaceId = 6403373529
        local secondPlaceId = 16034567693
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        local function executeAdminScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then
                game.Loaded:Wait()
            end

            if getgenv().AutoGetAdminExecuted == true then return end
            getgenv().AutoGetAdminExecuted = true

            if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                task.wait(10)
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(502, 76, 59)
                end
                task.wait(10)
                if getconnections then
                    for i,v in next, getconnections(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Idled) do
                        v:Disable() 
                    end
                else
                    while task.wait(10) do
                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Jump = true
                        end
                    end
                end

            elseif game.PlaceId == firstPlaceId then
                if game.ReplicatedStorage.Assets:FindFirstChild("Retro") then
                    game.ReplicatedStorage.Assets.Retro.Parent = workspace
                end
                repeat task.wait(10) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Retro")
                task.wait(10)
                for i,v in pairs(workspace.Retro.Map.RetroObbyMap:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.Name == "Model" and v:FindFirstChild("StaffApp") and v.StaffApp:FindFirstChild("Button") and v.StaffApp.Button:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v.StaffApp.Button.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,50,0)
                            task.wait(10)
                            fireclickdetector(v.StaffApp.Button.ClickDetector)
                        end
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local adminScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then
                            game.Loaded:Wait()
                        end
                        task.wait(10)
                        
                        local secondPlaceId = 16034567693
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                            task.wait(10)
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(502, 76, 59)
                            end
                            task.wait(10)
                            if getconnections then
                                for i,v in next, getconnections(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Idled) do
                                    v:Disable() 
                                end
                            else
                                while task.wait(10) do
                                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Jump = true
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    ]]

                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(adminScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(adminScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        if currentPlaceId == firstPlaceId or currentPlaceId == secondPlaceId then
            executeAdminScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(firstPlaceId)
            end)
            if not success and connection then
                connection:Disconnect()
            end
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Joust:AddButton({
    Title = "Someone Using Joust?",
    Callback = function()
        local found = false

        for _, player in ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "Joust" then
                    found = true
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Detected!",
                        Content = player.Name .. " has equipped the Joust glove.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                end
            end
        end

        if not found then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "No one has equipped the Joust glove",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Joust:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Joust Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Joust" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))

            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Duration = 3
            })
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Joust Player Not Found",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

    Title = "Auto Parry (Ability)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        getgenv().AutoGeneralAbility2s = Value

        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while getgenv().AutoGeneralAbility2s and task.wait(2) do
                    pcall(function()
                        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GeneralAbility:FireServer()
                    end)

            end)
        end
    end

local AutoLabyrinthToggle = Tabs.Run:AddToggle("AutoLabyrinth", {
    Title = "Auto Touch Labyrinth Doors",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AutoLabyrinth = Value
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local char = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
        local hrp = char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")

        while _G.AutoLabyrinth do
            for _, labyrinth in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                if string.find(labyrinth.Name, "Labyrinth") and labyrinth:FindFirstChild("Doors") then
                    for _, door in ipairs(labyrinth.Doors:GetChildren()) do
                        local hitbox = door:FindFirstChild("Hitbox")
                        if hitbox and hitbox:IsA("BasePart") and hitbox:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TouchTransmitter") then
                            hrp.CFrame = hitbox.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                            firetouchinterest(hrp, hitbox, 0)
                            task.wait(0.1)
                            firetouchinterest(hrp, hitbox, 1)
                            task.wait(0.3)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            task.wait(0.5)
        end
    end
})

    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
            repeat task.wait()
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(289, 13, 261)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").DigEvent:FireServer({["index"] = 2,["cf"] = CFrame.new(42.7222366, -6.17449856, 91.5175781, -0.414533257, 1.72594355e-05, -0.91003418, -5.57037238e-05, 1, 4.4339522e-05, 0.91003418, 6.90724992e-05, -0.414533257)})
            until game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("TreasureChestFolder") ~= nil and game.Workspace.TreasureChestFolder:FindFirstChild("TreasureChest") ~= nil
            wait(1)
            game.Workspace.TreasureChestFolder.TreasureChest.OpenRemote:FireServer()
            wait(0.9)
            game.ReplicatedStorage.HumanoidDied:FireServer(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character,false)
            wait(3.75)
            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.BountyHunterRoom.BountyHunterBooth._configPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(-5,0,0)
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Accept Quest/Enter Arena First",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end

            ReplicatedStorage.bob:FireServer()

Tabs.Knockoff:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Get Knockoff Glove",
    Callback = function()
        local buttonsToPress = {4, 5, 5, 3, 2, 9, 3}
        local foundRoom = false

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            local character = player.Character
            if character and character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
                local roomName = player.Name .. "'s Room"
                local room = workspace.RoomsFolder:FindFirstChild(roomName)

                if room and room:FindFirstChild("PocketKeypad") then
                    local keypad = room.PocketKeypad
                    local buttons = keypad:FindFirstChild("Buttons")

                    if buttons then
                        foundRoom = true

                        for _, num in ipairs(buttonsToPress) do
                            local button = buttons:FindFirstChild(tostring(num))
                            if button then
                                local cd = button:FindFirstChildOfClass("ClickDetector")
                                if cd then
                                    fireclickdetector(cd)
                                    wait(0.15)
                                end
                            end
                        end

                        local enterButton = buttons:FindFirstChild("Enter")
                        if enterButton then
                            local cd = enterButton:FindFirstChildOfClass("ClickDetector")
                            if cd then
                                fireclickdetector(cd)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        if not foundRoom then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "No one is in the arena!",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Frostbite Tab
Tabs.Frostbite:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Ice Trials Place + Get Ice Essence",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 17290438723
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        local function executeItemScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then
                game.Loaded:Wait()
            end

            game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                Title = "Credits to Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                Text = "Made by @nexer1234 ( youtube & discord )",
                Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                Duration = 36000,
                Button1 = "Thanks!"
            })

            game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                Title = "Message from Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                Text = "Please re-execute script after teleporting",
                Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                Duration = 36000,
                Button1 = "Oh..."
            })

            if game.PlaceId == 17290438723 then
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-555, 180, 55)
                wait(1)
                for i,v in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v.ClassName == "ProximityPrompt" then
                        if v.HoldDuration ~= 0 then
                            v.HoldDuration = 0
                        end
                        if v.RequiresLineOfSight ~= false then
                            v.RequiresLineOfSight = false
                        end
                        if v.MaxActivationDistance ~= 9e9 then
                            v.MaxActivationDistance = 9e9
                        end
                        v.Enabled = true
                        fireproximityprompt(v)
                    end
                end

            elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(17290438723) end
            else
                game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                    Title = "Message from Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                    Text = "Wrong game buddy",
                    Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                    Duration = 36000,
                    Button1 = "Oh..."
                })
            end
        end

        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local itemScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then
                            game.Loaded:Wait()
                        end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == 17290438723 then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-555, 180, 55)
                            wait(1)
                            for i,v in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if v.ClassName == "ProximityPrompt" then
                                    if v.HoldDuration ~= 0 then
                                        v.HoldDuration = 0
                                    end
                                    if v.RequiresLineOfSight ~= false then
                                        v.RequiresLineOfSight = false
                                    end
                                    if v.MaxActivationDistance ~= 9e9 then
                                        v.MaxActivationDistance = 9e9
                                    end
                                    v.Enabled = true
                                    fireproximityprompt(v)
                                end
                            end
                        elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                            while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(17290438723) end
                        end
                    ]]

                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(itemScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(itemScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            executeItemScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId)
            end)
            if not success and connection then
                connection:Disconnect()
            end
        end
    end
})

            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(8, 97, 4)

            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Fortlol:FireServer()
            wait(3.5)
            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = false
            wait(0.1)
            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(8, 106, -6)
            wait(0.5)
            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = OGL
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Fort",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end

Tabs.Spoonful:AddButton({

Tabs.Spoonful:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Place Tycoon",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Tycoon" then
            wait(0.1)
            local button = script.Parent
            local teleportPosition = Vector3.new(-910, 328, 2)

            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(teleportPosition)
            end
            wait(0.1)
            local button = script.Parent
            local teleportPosition = Vector3.new(17884, -24, -3539)

            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(teleportPosition)
            end
            wait(0.1)
            local args = {
                [1] = CFrame.new(17893.552734375, -26.257728576660156, -3535.35888671875, 0.00862560048699379, 3.3499091500743816e-08, -0.9999628067016602, 8.43312697451637e-10, 1, 3.350761090814558e-08, 0.9999628067016602, -1.1323045834288337e-09, 0.00862560048699379)
            }

            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("GeneralAbility"):FireServer(unpack(args))
            wait(0.1)
            while true do
                local part = workspace:WaitForChild("┬áTycoonhacedgame3")
                local clickDetector = part:WaitForChild("Click").ClickDetector

                local function fireClickForPlayer(player)
                    clickDetector:Fire(player)
                end

                game.Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(player)
                    part.Touched:Connect(function(hit)
                        local character = hit.Parent
                        if character:IsA("Model") and character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                            fireClickForPlayer(player)
                        end
                    end)
                end)
                wait()
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Tycoon",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

local SpoonfulAutoTycoonToggle = Tabs.Spoonful:AddToggle("SpoonfulAutoTycoon", {
    Title = "Auto Click Tycoon",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AutoTycoon = Value

        while _G.AutoTycoon do
            for _, v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                if string.find(v.Name, "ÅTycoon") then
                    local clickPart = v:FindFirstChild("Click")
                    if clickPart and clickPart:IsA("BasePart") then
                        local detector = clickPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("ClickDetector")
                        if detector then
                            fireclickdetector(detector)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end

-- Siphon Tab
local G_ = {}
G_.SiphonAuto = false

local SiphonAutoToggle = Tabs.Siphon:AddToggle("SiphonAuto", {
    Title = "Auto Bring Siphon Orb",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        G_.SiphonAuto = Value
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

        if G_.SiphonAuto then
            if player.leaderstats.Slaps.Value >= 0 then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while G_.SiphonAuto do
                        for _, v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                            if v.Name == "SiphonOrb" then
                                local head = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                                if head then
                                    firetouchinterest(head, v, 0)
                                    firetouchinterest(head, v, 1)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                end)
            else
                G_.SiphonAuto = false
                Fluent:Notify({
                    Title = "Error",
                    Content = "0+ Slaps Required",
                    Duration = 3
                })
            end
        end
    end
})

-- Wrench Tab
Tabs.Wrench:AddButton({
    Title = "Equip Engineer (9k+ Slaps Need)",
    Callback = function()
        fireclickdetector(workspace.Lobby["Engineer"].ClickDetector)
    end
})

Tabs.Wrench:AddButton({
    Title = "Someone Using Thor?",
    Callback = function()
        local found = false

        for _, player in ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "Thor" then
                    found = true
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Detected!",
                        Content = player.Name .. " has equipped the Thor glove.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                end
            end
        end

        if not found then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "No one has equipped the Thor glove",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Wrench:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Thor Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Thor" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))

            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Duration = 3
            })
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Thor Player Not Found",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Wrench:AddButton({
    Title = "Spawn Sentry",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Engineer" then
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Sentry:FireServer()
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Engineer Glove",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Wrench:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Turret",
    Callback = function()
        local turret = game.workspace:FindFirstChild("Turret")
        if turret and turret:FindFirstChild("HingePart") and turret.HingePart:FindFirstChild("Glove") then
            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = turret.HingePart.Glove.CFrame
        end
    end
})

            if not game:IsLoaded() then

                DontGetAvatar = true

                if DontGetAvatar == true then

                    if not game:IsLoaded() then
                        game.Loaded:Wait()
                    end
                    wait(5)
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace["Big Heart"].CFrame
                    if not game:IsLoaded() then
                        game.Loaded:Wait()
                    end
                    wait(5)
                end
            end

            game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{

            game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{

                Text = "Please re-execute script after teleporting",

                Duration = 36000,

            })

            if game.PlaceId == 18550498098 then
                Checkamogus()
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(3258, -62, 824)

                    game.Loaded:Wait()

                wait(5)
                for i,v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v.Name == "ShackLever" and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector") then
                        fireclickdetector(v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                    end
                end
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(3258, -62, 824)
                if not game:IsLoaded() then
                    game.Loaded:Wait()
                end
                repeat task.wait(.1) until workspace.Map.Components:FindFirstChild("GuideNPC")
                task.wait(.8)
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(599, 250, -322)
                task.wait(.8)
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = true

                while task.wait(.1) do
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Lantern") then
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack.Lantern.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                    end

                    for i,v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                        if v.Name == "PusherWall" then
                            v.CanCollide = false
                        end

                        if v.Name == "DungeonGolem" and v:FindFirstChild("Cube.001") then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v["Cube.001"])
                            end
                        end

                        if v.Name == "golem" and v:FindFirstChild("Hitbox") then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.Hitbox)
                            end
                        end

                        if v.Name == "ReplicaNPC" and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.HumanoidRootPart)
                            end
                        end

                        if v.Name == "GuideNPC" and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.HumanoidRootPart)
                            end

                        if v.Name == "TrackGloveMissile" then

                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end

            elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                Instance.new("Message",game.CoreGui).Text = "You're being teleported, please wait, it may take up to a minute..."

        end

        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            executeItemScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId)
            end)
            if not success and connection then
                connection:Disconnect()
            end
        end
    end
})

-- Relude Tab
Tabs.Relude:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Guide Place + Get Relude Glove",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 18550498098
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        local function executeItemScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then
                game.Loaded:Wait()
            end

            function Checkamogus()
                DontGetAvatar = false
                repeat task.wait() until DontGetAvatar ~= nil

                if DontGetAvatar == true then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(3258, -65, 824)
                    if not game:IsLoaded() then
                        game.Loaded:Wait()
                    end
                    wait(5)
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace["the cube of life"].Part.CFrame
                    if not game:IsLoaded() then
                        game.Loaded:Wait()
                    end
                    wait(5)
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace["Big Heart"].CFrame
                    if not game:IsLoaded() then
                        game.Loaded:Wait()
                    end
                    wait(5)
                end
            end

            game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                Title = "Credits to Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                Text = "Made by @nexer1234 ( youtube & discord )",
                Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                Duration = 36000,
                Button1 = "Thanks!"
            })

            game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                Title = "Message from Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                Text = "Please re-execute script after teleporting",
                Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                Duration = 36000,
                Button1 = "Oh..."
            })

            if game.PlaceId == 18550498098 then
                Checkamogus()
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(3258, -62, 824)
                if not game:IsLoaded() then
                    game.Loaded:Wait()
                end
                wait(5)
                for i,v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v.Name == "ShackLever" and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector") then
                        fireclickdetector(v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                    end
                end
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(3258, -62, 824)
                if not game:IsLoaded() then
                    game.Loaded:Wait()
                end
                repeat task.wait(.1) until workspace.Map.Components:FindFirstChild("GuideNPC")
                task.wait(.8)
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(599, 250, -322)
                task.wait(.8)
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = true

                while task.wait(.1) do
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Lantern") then
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack.Lantern.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                    end
                    game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.Data.AnswerInCutscene:FireServer("Spare")

                    for i,v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                        if v.Name == "PusherWall" then
                            v.CanCollide = false
                        end

                        if v.Name == "DungeonGolem" and v:FindFirstChild("Cube.001") then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v["Cube.001"])
                            end
                        end

                        if v.Name == "golem" and v:FindFirstChild("Hitbox") then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.Hitbox)
                            end
                        end

                        if v.Name == "ReplicaNPC" and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.HumanoidRootPart)
                            end
                        end

                        if v.Name == "GuideNPC" and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.HumanoidRootPart)
                            end
                        end

                        if v.Name == "TrackGloveMissile" then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end

            elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                Instance.new("Message",game.CoreGui).Text = "You're being teleported, please wait, it may take up to a minute..."

                for i,v in pairs(workspace.BountyHunterRoom:GetChildren()) do
                    if v and v:IsA('Model') and v:FindFirstChild('Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005') then
                        if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].PlayerCounter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "0/4 Hunters" then
                            if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text ~= "1" then
                                repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "1"
                            end
                            while task.wait() do game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Hitbox.CFrame end
                        else
                            repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].PlayerCounter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "0/4 Hunters"
                            if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text ~= "1" then
                                repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "1"
                            end
                            while task.wait() do game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Hitbox.CFrame end
                        end
                    end
                end
            else
                game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                    Title = "Message from Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                    Text = "Wrong game buddy",
                    Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                    Duration = 36000,
                    Button1 = "Oh..."
                })
            end
        end

        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local itemScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then
                            game.Loaded:Wait()
                        end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        function Checkamogus()
                            DontGetAvatar = false
                            repeat task.wait() until DontGetAvatar ~= nil

                            if DontGetAvatar == true then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(3258, -65, 824)
                                if not game:IsLoaded() then
                                    game.Loaded:Wait()
                                end
                                wait(5)
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace["the cube of life"].Part.CFrame
                                if not game:IsLoaded() then
                                    game.Loaded:Wait()
                                end
                                wait(5)
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace["Big Heart"].CFrame
                                if not game:IsLoaded() then
                                    game.Loaded:Wait()
                                end
                                wait(5)
                            end
                        end

                        if game.PlaceId == 18550498098 then
                            Checkamogus()
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(3258, -62, 824)
                            if not game:IsLoaded() then
                                game.Loaded:Wait()
                            end
                            wait(5)
                            for i,v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if v.Name == "ShackLever" and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector") then
                                    fireclickdetector(v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                                end
                            end
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(3258, -62, 824)
                            if not game:IsLoaded() then
                                game.Loaded:Wait()
                            end
                            repeat task.wait(.1) until workspace.Map.Components:FindFirstChild("GuideNPC")
                            task.wait(.8)
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(599, 250, -322)
                            task.wait(.8)
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = true

                            while task.wait(.1) do
                                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Lantern") then
                                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack.Lantern.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                                end
                                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.Data.AnswerInCutscene:FireServer("Spare")

                                for i,v in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                                    if v.Name == "PusherWall" then
                                        v.CanCollide = false
                                    end

                                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v["Cube.001"])
                                        end
                                    end

                                    if v.Name == "golem" and v:FindFirstChild("Hitbox") then
                                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Lantern") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:FindFirstChild("Network") then
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.Hitbox)

                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v.HumanoidRootPart)

                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    ]]

                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(itemScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(itemScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            executeItemScript()

            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")

                TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId)
            end)

                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern:Activate()
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Lantern.Network:FireServer("Hit", v)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                            Instance.new("Message",game.CoreGui).Text = "You're being teleported, please wait, it may take up to a minute..."

                            for i,v in pairs(workspace.BountyHunterRoom:GetChildren()) do
                                if v and v:IsA('Model') and v:FindFirstChild('Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005') then
                                    if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].PlayerCounter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "0/4 Hunters" then
                                        if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text ~= "1" then
                                            repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "1"
                                        end
                                        while task.wait() do game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Hitbox.CFrame end
                                    else
                                        repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].PlayerCounter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "0/4 Hunters"
                                        if v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text ~= "1" then
                                            repeat task.wait(.1) until v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Counter.SurfaceGui.TextLabel.Text == "1"
                                        end
                                        while task.wait() do game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v["Meshes/boxshadow_Cube.005"].Hitbox.CFrame end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    ]]

                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(itemScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(itemScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            executeItemScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId)
            end)
            if not success and connection then
                connection:Disconnect()
            end
        end
    end
})
