-- Fan Tab
Tabs.Fan:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Teleport To barzil Place + Get Fan",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 7234087065
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        local function executeFanScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end

            game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                Title = "Credits to Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                Text = "Made by @nexer1234 ( youtube & discord )",
                Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                Duration = 36000,
                Button1 = "Thanks!"
            })

            if game.PlaceId == 7234087065 then
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.QuestStuff.Key.CFrame
                task.wait(1.5)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.SuitUpClown:FireServer()
                task.wait(.25)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.KeyQuest:FireServer()
                task.wait(.25)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.KeyAcquired:FireServer()
                task.wait(.25)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.GOHOME:FireServer()
                task.wait(.25)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.KeyBadgeReward:FireServer()
                task.wait(1.5)
            elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(7234087065) end
            else
                game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                    Title = "Message from Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                    Text = "Wrong game buddy",
                    Icon = "rbxassetid://125704683916878",
                    Duration = 36000,
                    Button1 = "Oh..."
                })
            end
        end

        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            executeFanScript()
        else
            local connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local fanScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        if game.PlaceId == 7234087065 then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.QuestStuff.Key.CFrame
                            task.wait(1.5)
                            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.SuitUpClown:FireServer()
                            task.wait(.25)
                            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.KeyQuest:FireServer()
                            task.wait(.25)
                            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.KeyAcquired:FireServer()
                            task.wait(.25)
                            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.GOHOME:FireServer()
                            task.wait(.25)
                            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").RemoteEvents.KeyBadgeReward:FireServer()
                        end
                    ]]
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then syn.queue_on_teleport(fanScript) else queue_on_teleport(fanScript) end
                end
            end)
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success = pcall(function() TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId) end)
            if not success and connection then connection:Disconnect() end
        end
    end
})

-- Boxer Tab
Tabs.Boxer:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Teleport To barzil Place + Get Boxer",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 7234087065
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        local function executeBoxerScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end

            if game.PlaceId == 7234087065 then
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(4231.26123046875, 3510.86376953125, 270.4519958496094)
                repeat task.wait(.1) until workspace:FindFirstChild("BoxingGloves")
                task.wait(1)
                fireclickdetector(workspace.BoxingGloves.ClickDetector)
            elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(7234087065) end
            end
        end

        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            executeBoxerScript()
        else
            local connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local boxerScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        if game.PlaceId == 7234087065 then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(4231.26123046875, 3510.86376953125, 270.4519958496094)
                            repeat task.wait(.1) until workspace:FindFirstChild("BoxingGloves")
                            task.wait(1)
                            fireclickdetector(workspace.BoxingGloves.ClickDetector)
                        end
                    ]]
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then syn.queue_on_teleport(boxerScript) else queue_on_teleport(boxerScript) end
                end
            end)
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success = pcall(function() TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId) end)
            if not success and connection then connection:Disconnect() end
        end
    end
})

local MaterializefarmToggle = Tabs.MATERIALIZE:AddToggle("Materializefarm", {
    Title = "Auto Bring MATERIALIZE Orb",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.Materializefarm = Value
        while _G.Materializefarm do
            for i,v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                if v.Name == "MATERIALIZEOrb" then
                    firetouchinterest(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Head"), v, 0)
                    firetouchinterest(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Head"), v, 1)
                end
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end
})

-- Bind Tab
Tabs.Bind:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Binded Maze Place + Get Bind",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 74169485398268
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        local function executeBindScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end

            if game.PlaceId == 74169485398268 then
                local time = tick()
                while tick() - time < 10 do task.wait() fireclickdetector(workspace.Orb:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector")) end
                while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(6403373529) end
            elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(74169485398268) end
            end
        end

        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId then
            executeBindScript()
        else
            local connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local bindScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        if game.PlaceId == 74169485398268 then
                            local time = tick()
                            while tick() - time < 10 do task.wait() fireclickdetector(workspace.Orb:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector")) end
                            while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(6403373529) end
                        end
                    ]]
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then syn.queue_on_teleport(bindScript) else queue_on_teleport(bindScript) end
                end
            end)
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success = pcall(function() TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId) end)
            if not success and connection then connection:Disconnect() end
        end
    end
})

-- Clock Tab
Tabs.Clock:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Teleport To FNAO Place (NOT AUTO GETS GLOVE)",
    Callback = function()
        local firstPlaceId = 6403373529
        local secondPlaceId = 7234087065
        local thirdPlaceId = 102908326578005
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        local function executeClockScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
            if getgenv().AutoGetClockExecuted then return end
            getgenv().AutoGetClockExecuted = true

            if game.PlaceId == thirdPlaceId then
                for i,v in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v.ClassName == "ClickDetector" then fireclickdetector(v) end
                end
                task.wait(2)
                for i,v in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v.ClassName == "ClickDetector" then fireclickdetector(v) end
                end
                task.wait(2)
                while task.wait() do
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(26.34327507019043, 4.055271148681641, -1.8455318212509155)
                    end
                end

            elseif game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(249.473419, 157.87326, -458.792145, 0.707134247, -0, -0.707079291, 0, 1, -0, 0.707079291, 0, 0.707134247)
                end
                task.wait(3)
                while task.wait() do
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                        for i,v in pairs(workspace.Buildings:GetChildren()) do
                            if v.Name == "wizard twoer" and v:FindFirstChild("Cone") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v.Cone.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,15,0)
                                break
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end

            elseif game.PlaceId == firstPlaceId or game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                while task.wait() do
                    game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(secondPlaceId)
                end
            end
        end

        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local clockScript = [[
                        getgenv().AutoGetClockExecuted = false
                        
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        local secondPlaceId = 7234087065
                        local thirdPlaceId = 102908326578005
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == thirdPlaceId then
                            for i,v in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if v.ClassName == "ClickDetector" then fireclickdetector(v) end
                            end
                            task.wait(2)
                            for i,v in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if v.ClassName == "ClickDetector" then fireclickdetector(v) end
                            end
                            task.wait(2)
                            while task.wait() do 
                                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(26.34327507019043, 4.055271148681641, -1.8455318212509155) 
                                end
                            end
                            
                        elseif game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(249.473419, 157.87326, -458.792145, 0.707134247, -0, -0.707079291, 0, 1, -0, 0.707079291, 0, 0.707134247)
                            end
                            task.wait(3)
                            while task.wait() do
                                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                    for i,v in pairs(workspace.Buildings:GetChildren()) do
                                        if v.Name == "wizard twoer" and v:FindFirstChild("Cone") then
                                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v.Cone.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,15,0)
                                            break
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    ]]

                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(clockScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(clockScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        if currentPlaceId == firstPlaceId or currentPlaceId == secondPlaceId or currentPlaceId == thirdPlaceId then
            executeClockScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(firstPlaceId)
            end)
            if not success and connection then
                connection:Disconnect()
            end
        end
    end
})

-- Angler Tab
Tabs.Angler:AddButton({
    Title = "Equip Lure (Catch Emm All Badge Need)",
    Callback = function()
        fireclickdetector(workspace.Lobby["Lure"].ClickDetector)
    end
})

Tabs.Angler:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Slap Aura Players",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Lure" then
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            while true do
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Leg") then
                        local args = {
                            [1] = player.Character["Left Leg"],
                            [2] = false
                        }
                        ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                    end
                end
                wait(0.5)
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Lure",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Jerry Tab
Tabs.Jerry:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Jerry Boss Fight Place + Auto Get Jerry",
    Callback = function()
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        if currentPlaceId == 6403373529 then
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            wait(0.2)
            local arena = workspace:FindFirstChild("Arena")
            if arena then
                local xmasSnowPeeps = arena:FindFirstChild("XmasSnowPeeps")
                if xmasSnowPeeps then
                    for _, peep in ipairs(xmasSnowPeeps:GetChildren()) do
                        if peep:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                            fireclickdetector(peep.ClickDetector)
                            wait(0.1)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            wait(0.2)
            if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(2, -5, 353)
            end

        elseif currentPlaceId == 95706409702231 then
            local function executeSecondPlaceScript()
                task.wait(20)
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-6, 21, -542)
                    _G.AntiAfk = true
                    local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
                    game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                        if _G.AntiAfk then
                            VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                            VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
                        end
                    end)

                    local bossManipulationThread = task.spawn(function()
                        while task.wait(0.01) do
                            local boss = workspace:FindFirstChild("Boss")
                            if boss and boss:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                                boss.Humanoid.Health = 1
                                task.wait(0.02)
                                boss.Humanoid.Health = 0
                            else
                                task.wait(1)
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    _G.BossManipulationThread = bossManipulationThread
                end
            end
            executeSecondPlaceScript()
        end

        game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
            if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                local targetPlaceId = 95706409702231
                local teleportScript = [[
                    wait(5)
                    if game.PlaceId == ]] .. targetPlaceId .. [[ then
                        task.wait(20)
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                            player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-6, 21, -542)
                            _G.AntiAfk = true
                            local VirtualUser = game:GetService('VirtualUser')
                            game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                                if _G.AntiAfk then
                                    VirtualUser:CaptureController()
                                    VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
                                end
                            end)

                            local bossManipulationThread = task.spawn(function()
                                while task.wait(0.01) do
                                    local boss = workspace:FindFirstChild("Boss")
                                    if boss and boss:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                                        boss.Humanoid.Health = 1
                                        task.wait(0.02)
                                        boss.Humanoid.Health = 0
                                    else
                                        task.wait(1)
                                    end
                                end
                            end)
                            _G.BossManipulationThread = bossManipulationThread
                        end
                    end
                ]]

                if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                    syn.queue_on_teleport(teleportScript)
                elseif queue_on_teleport then
                    queue_on_teleport(teleportScript)
                end
            end
        end)
    end
})

-- Snowroller Tab
Tabs.Snowroller:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Teleport To A Bad Dream Place (NOT AUTO GETS GLOVE)",
    Callback = function()
        local targetPlaceId = 92516899071319
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        local function executeSnowrollerScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end

            if game.PlaceId == 92516899071319 then
                workspace:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact").Handle.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                task.wait(1)
                repeat task.wait() if workspace:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact") then workspace:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact").Handle.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame end until workspace:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact") == nil
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact") then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact").Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                    repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact")
                end
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact"):Activate()
            elseif game.PlaceId == 118650724506449 then
                for i = 1, 10 do
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(54,50,196)
                        workspace.rooms["room exit"].EXIT.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                        task.wait(.5)
                    end
                end
                game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(6403373529)
            end
        end

        if currentPlaceId == targetPlaceId or currentPlaceId == 118650724506449 then
            executeSnowrollerScript()
        else
            local connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local snowrollerScript = [[
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        if game.PlaceId == 92516899071319 then
                            workspace:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact").Handle.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                            task.wait(1)
                            repeat task.wait() if workspace:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact") then workspace:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact").Handle.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame end until workspace:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact") == nil
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact").Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                                repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact")
                            end
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Unstable Artifact"):Activate()
                        elseif game.PlaceId == 118650724506449 then
                            for i = 1, 10 do
                                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(54,50,196)
                                    workspace.rooms["room exit"].EXIT.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                                    task.wait(.5)
                                end
                            end
                            game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(6403373529)
                        end
                    ]]
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then syn.queue_on_teleport(snowrollerScript) else queue_on_teleport(snowrollerScript) end
                end
            end)
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success = pcall(function() TeleportService:Teleport(targetPlaceId) end)
            if not success and connection then connection:Disconnect() end
        end
    end
})

-- Mouse Tab
Tabs.Mouse:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Cheese Place + Get Mouse",
    Callback = function()
        local firstPlaceId = 6403373529
        local secondPlaceId = 97220865182663
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        local function executeMouseScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
            if getgenv().AutoGetMouseExecuted then return end
            getgenv().AutoGetMouseExecuted = true

            if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                if workspace.Game.Buildings.City:FindFirstChild("City") == nil then
                    game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.PlaceBuilding:FireServer("City", Vector3.new(3.125, 43.4450798034668, -57.1875), 0)
                end

                while task.wait(.003) do
                    for i,v in pairs(workspace.Game.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                        if v.Name == "Rat" and v:FindFirstChild("Hitbox") and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid") and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").Health ~= 0 then
                            v.Hitbox.Anchored = true
                            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.GloveHit:FireServer(v.Hitbox)
                            v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").Health = 0
                        end
                    end
                    game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.UnlockGloveWithOrbs:FireServer()
                end

            elseif game.PlaceId == firstPlaceId or game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") == nil then
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Slaps.Value >= 11500 then
                        fireclickdetector(workspace.Lobby["el gato"].ClickDetector)
                        repeat task.wait(.1) until game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "el gato"
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Lobby["Teleport1"].CFrame
                        repeat task.wait(.1) until game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        task.wait(.1)
                        fireclickdetector(workspace.Cheese.ClickDetector)
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local mouseScript = [[
                        getgenv().AutoGetMouseExecuted = false
                        
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        local secondPlaceId = 97220865182663
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                            if workspace.Game.Buildings.City:FindFirstChild("City") == nil then
                                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.PlaceBuilding:FireServer("City", Vector3.new(3.125, 43.4450798034668, -57.1875), 0)
                            end
                            while task.wait(.003) do
                                for i,v in pairs(workspace.Game.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
                                    if v.Name == "Rat" and v:FindFirstChild("Hitbox") and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid") and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").Health ~= 0 then
                                        v.Hitbox.Anchored = true
                                        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.GloveHit:FireServer(v.Hitbox)
                                        v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").Health = 0
                                    end
                                end
                                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.UnlockGloveWithOrbs:FireServer()
                            end
                        end
                    ]]
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(mouseScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(mouseScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        if currentPlaceId == firstPlaceId or currentPlaceId == secondPlaceId then
            executeMouseScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(firstPlaceId)
            end)
            if not success and connection then
                connection:Disconnect()
            end
        end
    end
})

-- Hexa Tab
Tabs.Hexa:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Teleport To White Place + Get Hexa",
    Callback = function()
        local firstPlaceId = 6403373529

                task.wait(5)
                fireclickdetector(workspace["Part 5"].Glove.Hitbox:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Finale") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                task.wait(5)
                fireclickdetector(workspace.Finale.Reward.Hitbox:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))

            elseif game.PlaceId == firstPlaceId or game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats and game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove and game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Obby" then
                    game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(secondPlaceId)
                else
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Error",
                        Content = "Equip Obby glove first!",
                        Duration = 5
                    })
                end
            end
        end

        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local hexaScript = [[
                        getgenv().AutoGetHexaExecuted = false
                        
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        local secondPlaceId = 98726100529621
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                            repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part I") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            task.wait(5)
                            workspace["Part I"].Obby["end"].CanCollide = false
                            workspace["Part I"].Obby["end"].CanTouch = true
                            workspace["Part I"].Obby["end"].CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                            repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part 2") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            task.wait(5)
                            workspace["Part 2"]["Adjacent Island"].PortalActivator.CanCollide = false
                            workspace["Part 2"]["Adjacent Island"].PortalActivator.CanTouch = true
                            workspace["Part 2"]["Adjacent Island"].PortalActivator.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                            repeat task.wait(.1) until workspace["Part 2"]:FindFirstChild("Portal")
                            workspace["Part 2"].Portal.CanCollide = false
                            workspace["Part 2"].Portal.CanTouch = true
                            workspace["Part 2"].Portal.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                            repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part 3") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            task.wait(5)
                            fireclickdetector(workspace["Part 3"].TpToNext.HitBox:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                            repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part 4") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            task.wait(5)
                            workspace["Part 4"].TPPart.CanCollide = false
                            workspace["Part 4"].TPPart.CanTouch = true
                            workspace["Part 4"].TPPart.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                            repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Part 5") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            task.wait(5)
                            fireclickdetector(workspace["Part 5"].Glove.Hitbox:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                            repeat task.wait(.2) until workspace:FindFirstChild("Finale") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            task.wait(5)
                            fireclickdetector(workspace.Finale.Reward.Hitbox:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                        end
                    ]]

                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(hexaScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(hexaScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        if currentPlaceId == firstPlaceId or currentPlaceId == secondPlaceId then
            executeHexaScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(firstPlaceId)
            end)
            if not success and connection then
                connection:Disconnect()
            end
        end
    end
})

        local targetPlaceId = 7234087065
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end

            if game.PlaceId == 136005148166028 then
                game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification",{
                    Title = "Message from Nexer1234_AnotherAlt",
                    Text = "Please don't move and don't touch anything!",

                })

                local Platform = (game.UserInputService.TouchEnabled and not game.UserInputService.MouseEnabled) and "Mobile" or "PC"
                fireclickdetector(workspace.Kitchen.Fridge.HitBox.ClickDetector)

                fireclickdetector(workspace.Kitchen.Fridge.GrantAward.ClickDetector)
                task.wait(1)
                fireclickdetector(workspace.Microwave.HitBox.ClickDetector)

                fireclickdetector(workspace.Microwave.HitBox.ClickDetector)

                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character["Brewzucki"]:Destroy()

                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:UnequipTools()
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Brewzucki") then

                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character["Brewzucki"]:Destroy()

                task.wait(5)
                local start = tick()

                        if v and v.Name:find("Popup_") then
                            v.Position = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.RealComputerScreenGui.ComputerScreen.SuggestionsQTE.RecyclingBin.Position

                task.wait(2)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.ComputerState:FireServer("Victory")
                task.wait(.25)
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.ComputerState:Destroy()
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.RealComputerScreenGui.Enabled = false
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false
                task.wait(1.5)
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-14,37,49)
                task.wait(2)
                repeat task.wait()
                    if Platform == "Mobile" then
                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.DavidShrineQTE.DavidShrineQTE.Mobile.SpawnArea:FindFirstChild("TapLabel") then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.DavidShrineQTE.DavidShrineQTE.Mobile.SpawnArea.TapLabel.Size = UDim2.new(10000, 0, 10000, 0)

                    elseif Platform == "PC" then
                        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.DavidShrineQTE.DavidShrineQTE.PC.QuickTimeLabel.Visible == true then
                            game:GetService("VirtualInputManager"):SendKeyEvent(true, game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.DavidShrineQTE.DavidShrineQTE.PC.QuickTimeLabel.Text, false, game:GetService("VirtualInputManager"))
                        end
                    end
                until game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.DavidShrineQTE.DavidShrineQTE.ScoreLabel.Text == "Score: 150"
            elseif game.PlaceId == 7234087065 then
                repeat task.wait() game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(250, 95, -62830) until workspace.Buildings:FindFirstChild("wizard twoer 2")
                task.wait(1.5)
                while task.wait() do
                    for i,v in pairs(workspace.Buildings["wizard twoer 2"]:GetChildren()) do
                        if v.Name == "Model" and v:FindFirstChild("Trigger") then
                            game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v:FindFirstChild("Trigger").CFrame
                        end
                    end
                end
            elseif game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 6403373529 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                while task.wait() do game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(7234087065) end
            end
        end

            executeMetaverseScript()
        else
            local connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then

-- Swordfighter Tab
Tabs.Swordfighter:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Sword Fight Place + Get Swordfighter",
    Callback = function()
        local firstPlaceId = 6403373529
        local secondPlaceId = 117232463555132
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        local function executeSwordfighterScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
            if getgenv().AutoGetSwordfighterExecuted == true then return end
            getgenv().AutoGetSwordfighterExecuted = true

            if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss.Head.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,10,0)
                end
                task.wait(3)
                if workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid") then
                    workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").RigType = "R15"
                    workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").Health = 0
                end
                repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.SkipButton.SkipDialogueButton.Visible == true
                task.wait()
                repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.SkipButton.SkipDialogueButton.Visible == false
                while task.wait() do
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Map.Components.GloveIsland.ClaimGlove.CFrame
                        if workspace.Map.Components.GloveIsland.ClaimGlove:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ProximityPrompt") then
                            fireproximityprompt(workspace.Map.Components.GloveIsland.ClaimGlove:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ProximityPrompt"))
                        end
                    end
                end

            elseif game.PlaceId == firstPlaceId or game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                for i,v in pairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:GetDescendants()) do
                    if v:IsA("BasePart") and v.CanCollide == true then
                        v.CanCollide = false
                    end
                end
                task.wait(.5)
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(316,40,196)
                end
                task.wait(1)
                game.ReplicatedStorage.RetroAbility:FireServer("Ban Hammer")
                task.wait(2)
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(310,34,191)
                end
                task.wait(2)
                game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(secondPlaceId)
            end
        end

        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local swordfighterScript = [[
                        getgenv().AutoGetSwordfighterExecuted = false
                        
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        local secondPlaceId = 117232463555132
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss.Head.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,10,0)
                            end
                            task.wait(3)
                            if workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid") then
                                workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").RigType = "R15"
                                workspace.Map.Components.NPCs.FinalBoss.FinalBoss:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid").Health = 0
                            end
                            repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.SkipButton.SkipDialogueButton.Visible == true
                            task.wait()
                            repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.SkipButton.SkipDialogueButton.Visible == false
                            while task.wait() do
                                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Map.Components.GloveIsland.ClaimGlove.CFrame
                                    if workspace.Map.Components.GloveIsland.ClaimGlove:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ProximityPrompt") then
                                        fireproximityprompt(workspace.Map.Components.GloveIsland.ClaimGlove:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ProximityPrompt"))
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    ]]
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(swordfighterScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(swordfighterScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        if currentPlaceId == firstPlaceId or currentPlaceId == secondPlaceId then
            executeSwordfighterScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(firstPlaceId)
            end)
            if not success and connection then
                connection:Disconnect()
            end
        end
    end
})

-- Tank Tab
Tabs.Tank:AddButton({
    Title = "Get Tank Glove",
    Callback = function()
        if game:GetService("BadgeService"):UserHasBadgeAsync(game.Players.LocalPlayer.UserId, 4390302507334168) and game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Slaps.Value >= 50000 then
            if not game.IsLoaded then
                game.Loaded:Wait()
            end

            _G.EquipGloveMethod = 1
            function EquipGlove(glove, time)
                glove = glove or "Default"
                time = time or 0.4
                task.wait()
                repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer and game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                task.wait()
                if _G.EquipGloveMethod == 1 then
                    if workspace.Lobby:FindFirstChild(glove) and workspace.Lobby[glove]:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector") then
                        if fireclickdetector or fireclickdetector() then
                            fireclickdetector(workspace.Lobby[glove].ClickDetector)
                            repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == glove
                            task.wait(time)
                        end
                    end
                elseif _G.EquipGloveMethod == 2 then
                    if workspace.Lobby:FindFirstChild(glove) then
                        for i,v in pairs(game.ReplicatedStorage._NETWORK:GetChildren()) do
                            if v and v.Name:find("{") or v.Name:match("{") and v:IsA("RemoteEvent") then
                                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == glove then
                                    break
                                end
                                v:FireServer(unpack({[1]=glove;}))
                                task.wait(time + .15)
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            function EnterPortal(portal, time)
                portal = portal or "Teleport1"
                time = time or 0.8
                task.wait()
                repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
                task.wait()
                if workspace.Lobby:FindFirstChild(portal) and workspace.Lobby[portal]:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Script") and game.Players.LocalPlayer and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") == nil then
                    old = workspace.Lobby[portal].CFrame
                    workspace.Lobby[portal].CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered")
                    workspace.Lobby[portal].CFrame = old
                    task.wait(time)
                end
            end
            function CheckGlove(glove)
                glove = glove or "Default"
                task.wait()
                repeat task.wait() until game.Players.LocalPlayer and game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("_unlockedGloves")
                task.wait()
                if game.Players.LocalPlayer._unlockedGloves:FindFirstChild(glove) then
                    return game.Players.LocalPlayer._unlockedGloves:FindFirstChild(glove).Value
                end
            end

            if CheckGlove("Shotgun") ~= true or CheckGlove("Pillow") ~= true then return end
            if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") == nil then
                EquipGlove("Pillow")
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GeneralAbility:FireServer(unpack({[1]=CFrame.new(17894.3867, -20.5577297, -3562.97974, 0.999158919, -1.34026186e-08, -0.04100601, 1.42693359e-08, 1, 2.08436735e-08, 0.04100601, -2.14112692e-08, 0.999158919);}))
                for i = 1, 200 do
                    game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Events.PillowEvent:FireServer("AddPillow")
                end
                task.wait(1)
                game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(17894.791, -23.6096096, -3577.8042, -0.999188364, 4.7269662e-08, 0.040281646, 4.80706674e-08, 1, 1.89165021e-08, -0.040281646, 2.08375148e-08, -0.999188364)
                task.wait(3)
                EquipGlove("Shotgun")
                repeat task.wait()
                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(17894.5547, -20.7577286, -3547.35376, 0.999844074, 3.9351038e-09, -0.0176601317, -3.07407322e-09, 1, 4.87827485e-08, 0.0176601317, -4.87208531e-08, 0.999844074)
                    game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GeneralAbility:FireServer("explosive")
                until workspace:FindFirstChild(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name.."'s PillowFort") == nil
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "You Dont Own Pillow/50k+ Slaps Required",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Eggler Tab
Tabs.Eggler:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Teleport To Egg Place + Get Eggler",
    Callback = function()
        local firstPlaceId = 6403373529
        local secondPlaceId = 129665246576996
        local currentPlaceId = game.PlaceId

        local function executeEgglerScript()
            if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
            if getgenv().AutoGetEgglerExecuted then return end
            getgenv().AutoGetEgglerExecuted = true

            if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                while task.wait() do
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                        game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(69,4240,2)
                    end
                    for i,v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                        if v and v.Name == "root" and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TouchTransmitter") then
                            v.CanCollide = false
                            v.CanTouch = true
                            v.CanQuery = true
                            v.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                        end
                    end
                    if workspace:FindFirstChild("Kenneth") and workspace.Kenneth:FindFirstChild("Head") and workspace.Kenneth.Head:FindFirstChild("ProximityPrompt") then
                        fireproximityprompt(workspace.Kenneth.Head.ProximityPrompt)
                    end
                end

            elseif game.PlaceId == firstPlaceId or game.PlaceId == 11520107397 or game.PlaceId == 9015014224 or game.PlaceId == 124596094333302 then
                for i,v in pairs(workspace.EasterHuntEggs:GetChildren()) do
                    if v and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector") then
                        fireclickdetector(v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector"))
                    end
                end
                repeat task.wait() until workspace:FindFirstChild("EggTeleport")
                task.wait()
                if workspace.EggTeleport and workspace.EggTeleport:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                    fireclickdetector(workspace.EggTeleport.ClickDetector)
                end
                task.wait(2)
                game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(secondPlaceId)
            end
        end

        local function setupTeleportMonitor()
            local connection
            connection = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.OnTeleport:Connect(function(state)
                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then
                    local egglerScript = [[
                        getgenv().AutoGetEgglerExecuted = false
                        
                        if not game:IsLoaded() then game.Loaded:Wait() end
                        task.wait(3)
                        
                        local secondPlaceId = 129665246576996
                        
                        if game.PlaceId == secondPlaceId then
                            while task.wait() do
                                if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                    game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(69,4240,2)
                                end
                                for i,v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                    if v and v.Name == "root" and v:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("TouchTransmitter") then
                                        v.CanCollide = false
                                        v.CanTouch = true
                                        v.CanQuery = true
                                        v.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                                    end
                                end
                                if workspace:FindFirstChild("Kenneth") and workspace.Kenneth:FindFirstChild("Head") and workspace.Kenneth.Head:FindFirstChild("ProximityPrompt") then
                                    fireproximityprompt(workspace.Kenneth.Head.ProximityPrompt)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    ]]
                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(egglerScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(egglerScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection
        end

        if currentPlaceId == firstPlaceId or currentPlaceId == secondPlaceId then
            executeEgglerScript()
        else
            local connection = setupTeleportMonitor()
            local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
            local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                TeleportService:Teleport(firstPlaceId)
            end)
            if not success and connection then
                connection:Disconnect()
            end
        end
    end
})

-- Silly Tab
Tabs.Silly:AddButton({
    Title = "Equip Baby (3750+ Slaps Need)",
    Callback = function()
        fireclickdetector(workspace.Lobby["Baby"].ClickDetector)
    end
})

Tabs.Silly:AddButton({
    Title = "Someone Using Fan?",
    Callback = function()
        local found = false

        for _, player in ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            local leaderstats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
            if leaderstats then
                local glove = leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if glove and glove.Value == "Fan" then
                    found = true
                    Fluent:Notify({
                        Title = "Detected!",
                        Content = player.Name .. " has equipped the Fan glove.",
                        Duration = 3
                    })
                end
            end
        end

        if not found then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "No one has equipped the Fan glove",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Silly:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Fan Player",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local foundPlayer = nil

        for _, player in pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= localPlayer then
                local stats = player:FindFirstChild("leaderstats")
                if stats and stats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and stats.Glove.Value == "Fan" then
                    foundPlayer = player
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if foundPlayer and foundPlayer.Character and foundPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            local hrp = foundPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
            localPlayer.Character:PivotTo(hrp.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))

            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success!",
                Content = "Teleported To: " .. foundPlayer.Name,
                Duration = 3
            })
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Fan Player Not Found",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

                game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(secondPlaceId)

                if state == Enum.TeleportState.InProgress then

                    if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
                        syn.queue_on_teleport(suctionScript)
                    else
                        queue_on_teleport(suctionScript)
                    end
                end
            end)
            return connection

        if currentPlaceId == firstPlaceId or currentPlaceId == secondPlaceId then
            executeSuctionScript()

Tabs.Bounty:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Slap Aura Players",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Hitman" then
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")

            while true do
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Leg") then
                        local args = {
                            [1] = player.Character["Left Leg"],
                            [2] = false
                        }
                        ReplicatedStorage.HitmanHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                    end
                end
                wait(0.5)
            end
        else
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Hitman",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Debug Tab
local debugCode = nil

Tabs.Debug:AddButton({
    Title = "Get Code",
    Callback = function()
        local code = ""

        local success1, duckCount = pcall(function()
            local ducks = workspace["Debug Room"].DuckTable.DuckTable:GetChildren()
            local count = 0
            for _, obj in ipairs(ducks) do
                if obj:IsA("MeshPart") and obj.Name == "Duck" then
                    count += 1
                end
            end
            return count
        end)
        code = code .. (success1 and tostring(duckCount) or "?")

        local success2, adminNum = pcall(function()
            local text = workspace["Debug Room"].AdminGloves.GlovesCode.SurfaceGui.AdminNumber.Text
            return tonumber(text) or 0
        end)
        code = code .. (success2 and tostring(adminNum) or "?")

        local success3, mazeNum = pcall(function()
            local text = workspace["Debug Room"].Maze.MazePrize.SurfaceGui.MazeNumber.Text
            return tonumber(text) or 0
        end)
        code = code .. (success3 and tostring(mazeNum) or "?")

        local success4, responseNum = pcall(function()
            local possiblePaths = {
                workspace:FindFirstChild("Rig"),
                workspace:FindFirstChild("Debug Room"),
                workspace:FindFirstChild("Map")
            }

            for _, location in ipairs(possiblePaths) do
                if location then
                    local dialog = location:FindFirstChild("Dialog")
                    if not dialog then
                        dialog = location:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Dialog")
                    end

                    if dialog then
                        local dialogChoices = dialog:GetChildren()
                        for _, choice in ipairs(dialogChoices) do
                            if choice:IsA("DialogChoice") then
                                local response = choice.ResponseDialog
                                if response then
                                    local found = string.match(response, "%d+")
                                    if found then
                                        return tonumber(found)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            return 0
        end)

        if not success4 or responseNum == 0 then
            local success5, altResponseNum = pcall(function()
                for _, dialog in ipairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                    if dialog:IsA("Dialog") then
                        for _, choice in ipairs(dialog:GetChildren()) do
                            if choice:IsA("DialogChoice") then
                                local response = choice.ResponseDialog
                                if response then
                                    local found = string.match(response, "%d+")
                                    if found then
                                        return tonumber(found)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                return 0
            end)

            if success5 and altResponseNum ~= 0 then
                responseNum = altResponseNum
                success4 = true
            end
        end

        code = code .. (success4 and tostring(responseNum) or "?")

        debugCode = code

        Fluent:Notify({
            Title = "Code Checker",
            Content = "The Debug Glove Code is: " .. code,
            Duration = 5
        })
    end
})

Tabs.Debug:AddButton({
    Title = "Claim Debug Glove",
    Callback = function()
        if not debugCode or string.find(debugCode, "?") then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Code not found or incomplete. Please run the first button again.",
                Duration = 4
            })
            return
        end

        local buttonsModel = workspace["Debug Room"].Keypad.Buttons

        for digit in debugCode:gmatch("%d") do
            local buttonPart = buttonsModel:FindFirstChild(digit)
            if buttonPart then
                local clickDetector = buttonPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("ClickDetector")
                if clickDetector then
                    fireclickdetector(clickDetector)
                    wait(0.2)
                end
            end
        end

        local enterPart = buttonsModel:FindFirstChild("Enter")
        if enterPart then
            local enterClick = enterPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("ClickDetector")
            if enterClick then
                fireclickdetector(enterClick)
            end
        end

        Fluent:Notify({
            Title = "Success",
            Content = "Code entered: " .. debugCode,
            Duration = 4
        })
    end
})

    Callback = function()
        fireclickdetector(workspace.Lobby["Scythe"].ClickDetector)
    end

Tabs.Conker:AddButton({
    Title = "Equip Snow (85+ Slaps Need)",
    Callback = function()
        fireclickdetector(workspace.Lobby["Snow"].ClickDetector)
    end
})

Tabs.Conker:AddButton({
    Title = "Auto Slap Aura Players",
    Callback = function()
        local gloveConfigs = {
            ["Rage"] = {
                remoteName = "GRRRR",
                action = function(player)
                    if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Leg") then
                        local args = {
                            [1] = player.Character["Left Leg"],
                            [2] = false
                        }
                        ReplicatedStorage.GRRRR:FireServer(unpack(args))
                    end
                end
            },
            ["Eggler"] = {
                remoteName = "GeneralHit",
                action = function(player)
                    if player.Character then
                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                        if targetPart then
                            local args = {
                                [1] = targetPart,
                                [2] = {}
                            }
                            ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end
                end
            },
            ["Fan"] = {
                remoteName = "GeneralHit",
                action = function(player)
                    if player.Character then
                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                        if targetPart then
                            local args = {
                                [1] = targetPart,
                                [2] = {}
                            }
                            ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end
                end
            },
            ["Scythe"] = {
                remoteName = "GeneralHit",
                action = function(player)
                    if player.Character then
                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                        if targetPart then
                            local args = {
                                [1] = targetPart,
                                [2] = {}
                            }
                            ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end
                end
            },
            ["Snow"] = {
                remoteName = "SnowHit",
                action = function(player)
                    if player.Character then
                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head")
                        if targetPart then
                            local args = {
                                [1] = targetPart,
                                [2] = {}
                            }
                            ReplicatedStorage.SnowHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end
                end
            }
        }

        local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
        local Players = game:GetService("Players")
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer

        local equippedGlove = localPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value

        if not gloveConfigs[equippedGlove] then
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Error",
                Content = "Equip one of: Rage, Eggler, Fan, Scythe, or Snow",
                Duration = 3
            })
            return
        end

        local gloveConfig = gloveConfigs[equippedGlove]

        while true do
            for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player ~= localPlayer then
                    gloveConfig.action(player)
                end
            end
            wait(0.5)
        end
    end
})

                    foundPlayer = player

                end

                Duration = 3
            })

    end

local WheelchairAntiRagdollToggle = Tabs.Wheelchair:AddToggle("WheelchairAntiRagdoll", {
    Title = "Anti Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AntiRagdoll = Value

        while _G.AntiRagdoll do
            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
            if char and char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                if char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled") and char.Ragdolled.Value == true then
                    local torso = char:FindFirstChild("Torso")
                    if torso then
                        torso.Anchored = true
                        repeat task.wait() until char.Ragdolled.Value == false
                        torso.Anchored = false
                    end
                end
            end
            task.wait()
        end
    end
})

    Title = "Anti Void",
    Callback = function()
        if workspace:FindFirstChild("AntiVoid") == nil then
            local Safespot = Instance.new("Part",workspace)
            Safespot.Name = "AntiVoid"
            Safespot.Position = Vector3.new(-51, -12, 108)
            Safespot.Size = Vector3.new(1000000, 1, 1000000)
            Safespot.Anchored = true
            Safespot.CanCollide = true
            Safespot.Transparency = .5
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success",
                Content = "Created Successfully!",
                Duration = 3
            })
        else
            game.workspace.AntiVoid:Destroy()
            Fluent:Notify({
                Title = "Success",
                Content = "Removed Successfully!",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Pinata:AddButton({
    Title = "Teleport To Oven",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local playerName = localPlayer.Name

        local ovenModel = workspace:FindFirstChild(playerName .. "'s Oven")

        if not ovenModel then
            for _, obj in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                if obj:IsA("Model") and obj.Name:find(playerName) and obj.Name:find("Oven") then
                    ovenModel = obj
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if not ovenModel then
            for _, obj in pairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                if obj:IsA("Model") and obj.Name:find("Oven") then
                    ovenModel = obj
                    break
                end
            end
        end

        if ovenModel then
            local hitbox = ovenModel:FindFirstChild("Hitbox")

            if not hitbox then
                hitbox = ovenModel:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
            end

            if hitbox then
                local character = localPlayer.Character
                if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                    character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = hitbox.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

Tabs.Pinata:AddButton({
    Title = "Place Birthday Cake",
    Callback = function()
        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer

        local cakeTool = nil
        for _, item in pairs(localPlayer.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
            if item:IsA("Tool") and item.Name == "Birthday Cake" then
                cakeTool = item
                break
            end
        end

        if cakeTool then
            localPlayer.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(cakeTool)
            task.wait(0.3)

            local success = false
            local island5 = workspace:FindFirstChild("Arena") and workspace.Arena:FindFirstChild("island5")

            if island5 then
                for _, part in pairs(island5:GetDescendants()) do
                    if part:IsA("BasePart") and part.Name == "Union.CakePromptPlacement" then
                        local prompt = part:FindFirstChild("CakeProximityPrompt")
                        if prompt and prompt:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
                            prompt:InputHoldBegin()
                            task.wait(0.1)
                            prompt:InputHoldEnd()
                            success = true
                            break
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
})
